Mr. Moon Sun-myung's Selected Words
43
Compilation Committee of Mr. Moon Sun-myung's Words

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Highest Summit
<Prayer> Today is the third Sabbath of April. Father, please remember the children gathered here. 
As your children welcome the spring season, grant them new news and new connections, 
and bestow abundant gifts upon those who have come seeking the light of new life. 
Please grant new grace to your beloved children gathered here, so that your wishes and joy may be revived in their hearts. 
Humans always need change and awareness. We understand that to be able to receive such stimulation, one must possess a heart of longing, admiration, and earnestness. Therefore, may we have a sincere heart before your will, and guide us to realize tomorrow's hope within today's living sphere. If we do not bring forth results today that can shine tomorrow, we know that it cannot serve as a stimulus or joy before you or ourselves, so please look after your prostrated children here. 
Humans are letting time pass by. They only know that one year goes by and another comes, but in the midst of that, ten years can pass, twenty years can pass, and one can let half a lifetime or an entire life slip away. We know that we must never stand in a position that betrays your will in this short life journey. 
We must understand that without the decisive effort of the Father, who walked the path of merciless struggle that we cannot even imagine, we cannot walk that path or have that connection. 
It is a thankful thing that today is digested in joy, but if we cannot carry this joy into tomorrow, we must understand that today's joy will become an eternal enemy to us, and can only be a condition of sorrow, difficulty, and lamentation. Joy is not only good, and sorrow is not only bad. The issue is how much inner struggle for the fulfillment of one's purpose connects joy and sorrow in one's environment. 
When we come to understand this, we will reflect on how much we have aligned with the will in our life journey, and how our joy and sorrow connect with the value of the will. The will governs our lives and governs eternal life and connections, and when we think about this, we realize that the will presides over not only today but also over the eternal historical era. 
When we think about the fact that the Father directly becomes the reality and observes and perceives this era as the historical center, we come to know that being in harmony with the central Father is joy, while being out of harmony and distancing ourselves is sorrow. 
Father, we must understand your sorrow. We must clearly know from what position you are calling us and what content you are seeking us with. Everything that comes and goes must not be planned in useless lines, so whether we live or die, we must go through the process of starting with a position that does not contradict your authority and reach the result. Since we must ultimately go before you in this current environment, may we discuss our entirety with you, receive advice from you, and prepare ourselves to match your final victory and support as a glory. 
We have come to know that the path of joy you must walk is intertwined with sorrow, and that the world of despair comes before the world of hope. When we think about the fact that we have not appeared before you as children of joy but as children of resentment who have left traces of sorrow and tears, we must clearly understand what the restoration journey you must walk is like. We must recognize that we, the Father, I, and the family, nation, and world are all placed before the judgment. 
We must understand that it is a habit for us to center ourselves when facing the will of heaven. If we cannot inherit the hopeful tradition due to our habits, we will inevitably be pushed out of the position of inheriting that tradition. 
More than today, tomorrow; more than tomorrow, the day after tomorrow. Through these days, we must continuously strive to align with your will and your lofty grace. May we become your sons and daughters who can feel this. 
Every time we kneel and pray before you, we come to realize that you do not call us from the place of joy but from the extreme place of suffering and pain. Since this is a providential path that we must walk while reaffirming tomorrow, the appearance that manifests today is a sorrowful one, and we must understand that your heart is a lonely one. Furthermore, we must truly understand that we must fulfill our filial duty before your will, which pursues the value of the object until the end. 
If there is someone who can endure receiving humiliation ten times rather than receiving praise ten times, he will surely become a happy son, and we must understand that he will inevitably become a son whom heaven cannot help but love. It is not the place where we receive praise ten times that becomes a blessing for us, nor is it where victory is assured. If we cannot become sons and daughters who can have great hope in their hearts without being troubled even after receiving rebuke more than ten times, we know that we cannot bear the great mission of world restoration. 
Father, we know that until now you have loved the Unification Church. You are in a position of direct love, but you cannot love your beloved sons and daughters without overcoming greater trials, and we know that the Unification Church is walking the path of suffering today. Since we are in a position where we must find the restoration journey amidst suffering that no one knows, we must understand that each of us has a stage to fight on this path. 
When you call from the homeland and ask, "How will you fight for the nation, and what center will you have to fight for the nation?" we must boldly prepare ourselves and step forward to respond, "Father, I have come for that will." 
When there is joy, humans always want to rejoice centered on themselves, and when there is sorrow, they always want to avoid it. Father, we may find ourselves in such a position due to personal circumstances, but when we think that there is a deeper difficulty and sorrow centered on the will, we must have a strong and courageous heart as we swear and go for the will. 
We must understand that rather than lamenting and criticizing the past path centered on our current selves, there are greater hurdles we must overcome. Rather than recalling something from the past, we should reflect on how much effort the Father has put in, forgetting our own sorrows and pains, and becoming sons and daughters who can worry about the Father’s sorrow and suffering. We sincerely hope and wish to become such sons and daughters. 
Father, please be with us today, and protect the children of unification scattered across the nation. We have a familial responsibility that we cannot avoid on behalf of this land. Blessed daughters representing families are on the front lines. This path was not created due to my personal circumstances. We know that it is a path of destiny that must be taken for the fate of the nation and the world. 
We know that the path Jesus walked is the path Christianity must take, and it is the path our descendants must walk. We learned that walking the path of the cross was not Jesus' desire through his prayers in the Garden of Gethsemane. When we think that because Jesus walked the path of shedding blood, even his closest disciples had to shed blood, we understand that the path of blood is the path of restoration. 
The path that the Unification Church has walked today is the same. We must clearly understand that because you walked such a path, the Unification Church must also walk that path of destiny. Because there are paths of trials for individuals, families, and tribes, we know that there are also paths of trials that individuals, families, and tribes must walk. 
We know that there is a destiny that must be centered on the family. Historically, there has never been a standard where individuals walked on behalf of families, nor a standard where they walked on behalf of nations. Therefore, we understand that we must know this path as a mission and must not fail to indemnify. We must understand that your beloved daughters of unification, who are placed in such a destiny, must not become unfilial daughters shedding tears of sorrow on the front lines. 
They must become filial daughters who serve you wholeheartedly, and with your grace and protection, they must be able to surpass their husbands and families, as well as their neighbors, relatives, and friends. 
It is not only that every member of our individual families has become an enemy, but there are also hurdles that must be overcome centered on the nation. We must clearly understand that such a tremendous restoration journey remains. 
Father, we have decided to walk this path, so we must follow it silently. Before rejoicing in what we have done today, we must worry about the sorrows that will come tomorrow, and we know that we must extend today’s joy by sharing it with the nation and the world. 
We have come to understand that this path cannot be followed by looking at anyone in the world. It is a path that recognizes only heaven as the Father, a path that must rely solely on the Father, and a path that must honor only the Father. Therefore, we must understand that no one can become our friend, and that even the closest people, including our spouses and children, cannot replace this work. 
Because our family members have become enemies, we know that those who block our paths and inflict wounds upon us are the closest people. We must understand that those who cause God to despair and push Him into a place of sorrow are also those who claim to believe in God. Therefore, we must become humble before you as we go, and we must become those who worry about your will as we proceed. 
Even if we must die a hundred or a thousand times, we know that it is our duty and mission to leave only your will behind on this restoration path. This body that has stepped forward for this will has sworn more than once. We know that the pledges of the Unification Church community, made a thousand or ten thousand times, will never be in vain. 
That pledge is made with our lives, and it is made in a place as sharp as a dagger, where one feels as if they are cutting off their own life. We must understand the difficult and harsh reality of being on the path of indemnity where we cannot help but go. 
In the face of such a solemn mission and task, we must make an internal determination to overcome sorrow on behalf of Jesus and must not fail to break through the present reality with hope. We must understand that this journey is the path of restoration and the path that the Father walks. 
Therefore, we must come to feel more and more that the only one who is pitiful is you, and that those who bear the name of sons and daughters of the Unification Church must clearly understand this. Those sons and daughters are not those born with the lineage of any ancestor but are those who have been harvested through the connection of heavenly principles or the merits of their ancestors' blood. 
We must understand that because we are such sons and daughters, we possess tremendous value. We must sincerely hope and wish to realize that we are the ones who must rise to the occasion before anyone else elevates us. 
Until now, you have led the Unification Church, so we must entrust all that is to come to you. We know that no one but you can guide us. We believe that you will lead us all, and as we follow your guidance, we know that the path you walk is the path of the cross. We understand that it is a path where the tears of blood have been accumulated repeatedly, and the more we look at that path, the more we realize that we cannot walk it without believing in you. 
We must understand that it is a path that cannot be walked by criticizing and asserting from our own standpoint, and that to walk that path, we must suffer losses today, suffer losses tomorrow, and suffer losses throughout our lives. When we think this way, we come to realize that the only one who is pitiful in this entire universe is the Father. 
If a parent has ten children, the parent must do well by all ten children for them to be happy. However, when we see that children often prefer things that are contrary to their parents, we must understand how lonely, miserable, and pitiful the Father, who has led billions of humanity until now, must be.
Heavenly Father, we know that your efforts and suffering in establishing your providential will while looking at humanity, which has a bloodline connection that is in stark contrast to yours, are immense. Yet, you have not driven us with a whip.

We must understand that to lead humanity to a place where we can call you Father with a heart of compliance and a heart of inspiration, we must go through the arduous path of trials and tribulations.

To enable us to call you Father, we must recognize how many tears of blood have been shed in the background by you, our Father, and we must not let that be in vain. When I think about standing in the providential will that others do not know today, I realize that behind it lie countless tears from eons, the crossroads of death, and the inheritance of the altar of blood. I come to understand that the path of your will is one that cannot be faced without tears. Father, how much have you labored to lead our church until now? I know that we must continue on today and tomorrow.

I understand that it is a human flaw to wish for everything to begin with oneself and to conclude with oneself. However, for the Unification Church, I have struggled to ensure that it does not conclude with oneself, but rather begins with the Father and must conclude with the Father. We must recognize that because you walked a path of misery, we too cannot escape the path of misery.

Knowing this path, even when the final misery reaches its peak, it is our destiny as the Unification Church to seek out the joy in you and to praise the glory of the Father. This is the mission of the children who are leading the Unification Church.

You know that I have sworn before you to live a life that does not owe a debt to others, and as time flows, and with the sorrowful fate of our nation in this present age, and with the calamities that will come upon Asia in the future, I think that the will of heaven must flow together with the world’s humanity that cannot find its way on the path of ultimate tragedy. Therefore, I know that you have established us.

Walking this path is akin to paving a highway; there are times when one must pay the price of death, and I realize that there are many hardships that one must face with the resolve to embrace death.

Until we have walked this entire path, we must maintain a sincere heart before the Father. When we call upon the Father, we must do so with a heart that melts our bones.

With such a heart, we must overcome the difficult circumstances of life. No matter what anyone says, we must endure, knowing the heart of the Father better than anyone else. We must humbly follow the Father and establish our connection as sons and daughters of the Father, and I sincerely hope that you will allow us to run until the end following you.

In 1971, I know that the day when all that is to come will be fulfilled is not far off. The fate of this nation is also gradually moving toward its final peak, so we must become the vanguard and the stepping stone here. When the time comes to govern this nation under your providence, we must know that you are looking for sons and daughters who can humbly respond, “Yes, I am here; please command me.”

We understand that all things are not accomplished merely by words but by pouring out our hearts, intentions, and sincerity. Those who are working to fulfill your will are not people who boast of themselves. They are not those who speak openly. They are those who act quietly, unnoticed by others, as if they have ears but cannot hear, mouths but cannot speak, and eyes but cannot see. We know that such people walk with you, Father. 

When we think about how history is opened through them and led by them, we earnestly hope and desire that you take charge of this church.

No one is the owner of this church. Since this church is the Unification Church that you have historically guided, it must go along with your destiny. We must leave traces of history as we go. We know that this path involves relentless battles. If there is a path of suffering and loneliness, may you, Father, carry on until the end.

When we think about complaining in front of our family with our own loneliness, we must remember that this is the nature of fallen humanity. We must recognize that Moses, who led Israel, was a great man. Abraham was great, and Noah was great as well. We must learn once again from the historical actions and lessons they walked.

Abraham received the command from the Father to leave his hometown of Ur of the Chaldeans and left without doubt. Noah received the command to build the ark for 120 years and did not doubt. Moses did not doubt during his 40 years in the wilderness of Midian. They had strong hearts of hope, and rather than doubt or resent the Father, they believed in the Father more and endured the difficult path.

We must remain steadfast on the path of endurance and be strong and courageous. I know that the path I take, resolved to go to the final place, is the path of restoration. We must decide what to do in the moment of negotiating our lives with the Father. This issue must be decided together with our children. We must resolve everything in front of our beloved wives, beloved parents, beloved relatives, and beloved nation and world, and we must become sons and daughters who can appreciate how difficult that path is.

If someone has made a mistake, it is not the fault of any one person, but ultimately the responsibility lies with the whole. When we take on this responsibility, we understand that we can return to the Father. Therefore, it is not a problem for each of us to be sad individually. It is not a problem for each of us to perish individually. The problem is that you are sad because of our individual sadness, and we understand well that this is the sorrow that is connected to you.

Father, we must understand that good and evil cannot stand in the same place. We know that in the path of the individual, it has been said that one’s family members can be enemies, and we understand that our family members may be in the position of enemies. This is true in familial terms, in church terms, and in terms of the nation as well.

When we look at the Unification Church, we know that there have been personal enemies, familial enemies, church enemies, national enemies, and even global enemies. We also know that such enemies do not only exist externally but also within the Unification Church itself. We must recognize that the enemy is first within ourselves and close to us. We must have the heart to ruthlessly cut off and overcome the enemies that are close to us.

As we walk this path, we must know that we cannot absolutely trust anyone, including our children or spouses, and we must understand that we cannot absolutely rely on them. Many groups have claimed to believe in you, but we must clearly understand that they cannot be related to this path. We must not believe in anyone other than you, exalt only you, rely only on you, and walk the path of restoration while consulting with you.

Before speaking of a third party, we must become those who speak our own words with the Father, and before evaluating a third party, we must first be able to evaluate ourselves. This is the tradition that the sons and daughters of unity must have.

I earnestly hope and desire that you personally take charge of all of April and beyond. I know that from April to August, our church will face repeated trials. We must understand that if there are no external trials, there will be trials within ourselves. To avoid this time of suffering, we must devote all our sincerity. We must humbly bow down before the Father.

I must ask myself once again if I truly loved the Father. I must check once again if the Father is on my side. I must reflect once again on whether I am living because of the Father. I must judge once again whether I have a purpose in life for the Father. I earnestly ask that you allow your children to be those who can walk the path of your will until the end, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.

<Words> In order for a person to achieve their purpose with conviction, they must go through a process of struggle. The greater the hope, the more opposing elements will obstruct the fulfillment of that hope. These elements do not absorb into me but push back, and they do not welcome me but try to push me away. We know that when we move toward a great purpose, there is a path of suffering proportional to that purpose.

Conditions for Success
Everyone decides to succeed. There is no one in the world who does not dream of success centered on a great purpose. Each individual dreams and moves forward to achieve their purpose, but very few actually accomplish it. Even if the purpose is national, we must understand that only after entering the final position can one represent that nation in a moment of victory.

When a nation is in a path of suffering, those who flow along with that suffering cannot achieve a great purpose before the nation. When a nation is in a path of suffering, we must block the historical environment that flows along with it and go against it. To go against it, it is not enough to go against a few people among thirty million; we must go against all thirty million before we can have a foundation for victory that leads the entire nation to a new purpose.

When looking at global issues, if someone is aiming for a global peak and tries to avoid the trials of global suffering, they will never reach the global peak. However, if the path of the peak arises because of me and I affirm that it is an inevitable destiny that exists with me, thinking that it is not someone else's destiny but my lifelong destiny, then even if others see that path as difficult, if I go first and digest it, making it a value of life, I will become a global person. If there is a nation that has been determined to fight for a year, two years, ten years, a hundred years, or even thousands of years, that nation will become a global nation, and if there is a state like that, that state will surely dominate the world.

We know the nation of Israel. Today, we understand that the Jewish people are a nation that has become a global issue. They have been a wandering people, a customer without a country for two thousand years. They have suffered from the baptism of bullets from numerous nations and have been trampled by the hooves of many enemy nations. However, they have preserved their integrity. They did not walk the path of suffering for their own sake. Their ideology is that of the chosen people. They walk the path of suffering, but in the end, they hope that the Messiah will come and pay the price for all their suffering on a global scale.

As you may know from the newspapers, behind the kibbutz system is a spiritual motivation, which is the ideology of the chosen people. As a nation without a country, they have faced suffering wherever they have been, but that suffering could not erase the ideology of the chosen people that flows in their bones. Even in such environments, they have reaffirmed their ideology of the chosen people, and before lamenting their loneliness on the difficult path, they have clung to God and struggled to walk the path of the chosen people.

We know well that in any field of the world today, the Jewish people are an issue. So how did the Jewish nation become what it is today? It is because they cannot become a heavenly nation if they avoid the path of global suffering. Therefore, we understand that this nation has walked a path of inevitable destiny that it cannot escape.

There has been no nation or individual in any country that has welcomed the Jews. Even now, we know that when Jews appear, everyone dislikes them. However, even when they are in an environment that is disliked, because of their ideology of the chosen people, they cannot disappear from that environment.

The Jewish people have grown up in an environment from which they could not escape for a long time. From that position, they have rejected all conditions of trials and have not assimilated into that environment. We must recognize that such a position has become a shortcut to approaching heaven.

Not all Jews are like this, but we must understand that the Jewish people have had a historical motivation to carry deep patriotism.

Because they have endured the path of suffering until the end while embracing heaven, we know that the Jewish people are in a realistic situation where they cannot help but be a problem in the world.

The Unification Church must walk for God and the world
In this regard, if the path of the Unification Church is for the purpose of achieving any individual goal, it will perish along with the individual. It will disappear along with the individual. If the path of the Unification Church desires to walk with the Han people of the Republic of Korea, then if the Han people perish, the purpose will also perish. Moreover, if it becomes a movement trying to center on a few Asian countries, then if those few Asian countries cannot take a position to lead the world from a victorious position in history, the path of the Unification Church will be blocked.

Today, the path of the Unification Church is not just for the Republic of Korea, nor just for Asia, nor just for the world. You must understand that it is a path for God. The path of the Unification Church has never been a path for any individual from the beginning; it has been a path for God. Since the motivation is God, it is a path for God.

You must understand that God started as a God of sorrow, not a God of joy. So when can God appear as a God of joy? If there is an environment where God can command from the boundary of any nation, He must not remain at that peak but must go beyond it. If He has represented one nation, He must gather that nation and add another nation, progressing step by step not only through the world but also through the spirit world. We must understand that this is the will of God. Until we completely pass through this path, God cannot avoid the path of suffering.

Because God Himself started in sorrow, until that path is fully walked...
You must understand that sadness remains. If a nation suffers that sadness, then God also suffers; if the world suffers, then God suffers as well. Not only in this earthly world but also in the spiritual realm, all the paths of suffering tied to countless spirits must be traversed by God as well. If we do not resolve these issues from a spiritual standpoint, God will not have a day to rejoice with the world.

During the time of the world wars, when Japan fell, Germany fell, and Italy fell, the countries that participated in the war among democratic nations were more miserable than any other nation and came out bearing a heavy burden of suffering. However, when they overcame to the end in the place of suffering and achieved victory in the war, that victory was not just for a specific nation. We know that the groups that participated, regardless of whether they were large or small nations, shared in the joy of victory on that day.

God's providence of restoration did not start with joy but with sadness. It was sown in sadness. Because it was sown in sadness, it did not grow in joy but in sadness. Because it was sown in tears, it must grow through tears. You must understand that because it was sown in an environment that traverses the path of death, it must advance from the place that promises the path of death.

From this perspective, the path that the Unification Church must take is not a path that only serves the Republic of Korea. It cannot go along with the fate of any Asian country. It must go for the world. Even if a nation or a people rejoices because their own hopes have been fulfilled, they cannot rejoice together with that joy. No matter how much a nation rejoices, rejoicing centered around that nation does not mean rejoicing centered around the world. Therefore, when it is said that it was only for that nation, the path of restoration is to transcend that joy and confront the world's sadness.

You must become a representative who inherits God's heart. Because it was sown in sadness, it must be reaped in sadness. You all know the principle that you reap what you sow. Because it was sown in sadness, it must be reaped in sadness.

When considering the question of when God can rejoice, even if there is a place where He can rejoice, He cannot rejoice in a position where a sad environment becomes one with Him. 

For example, if parents are in difficulty, and there is a child who respects those struggling parents and tries to suffer alongside them, the parent, even without money, will have compassion when looking at that child who wishes to share in their hardships. Such a position connects to a place where new hopes can be promised. However, if a child goes out to a place of joy without knowing the sadness of their parents, there can be no unity of purpose there.

If a child can go to a place where they can be sadder than their parents while their parents are in a place of sadness, that child will establish a new historical connection with those parents. Parents give everything. Parents forgive children who are in a place of sadness with them. They say, "My child, keep this heart until you die!" As one grows older, it is not about abandoning this heart but rather about hoping for a deeper, higher, and broader sadness to join in the path of suffering. You must understand that this is the heart of parents.

Why is that? It is to give everything. It is to give everything to prevent greater suffering that is to come. Such parents will vow to face suffering greater than their own and will consider the path of suffering as their life, seeking children who can pledge to transcend the world's sadness centered around the sadness of their parents. When we think of this heart of parents in a sad position, we must understand that God is the same.

Because it was sown in sadness, we, who are walking the path of destiny, must receive God's comfort and go joyfully for ourselves; this is not for God. We must have the heart to comfort sad parents and to go to a place where we can be sadder than them, and we must make such movements, resolutions, or vows. Thus, we must comfort God and stimulate Him to look forward to tomorrow's hope and to overcome the current age of tribulation. Such matters are the same in the relationship between God and fallen human parents and children.

Until now, history has started in sadness, and we must develop a history of sadness and go to the ultimate end and the highest peak that will follow. You must understand that this is the path God must take.

Those who rejoice centered around their own individual selves, eating, crying, and pursuing only their own happiness will inevitably face disconnection. Such people will see the end. The issue is not about the ultimate peak we must reach. The issue is from where we inherit the ultimate peak and how we connect the path of the ultimate peak. You must understand that because God started in sadness, He must also reap in sadness.

When has there been a joyful day for God? Even if there are people in the world who know His will and rejoice and dance, they must understand God's sadness and step forward, shedding tears and overcoming loneliness to comfort God. Knowing that God hoped for such a place, it is through those who struggle to walk that path of suffering that God gains new hope.

Faith that empathizes
God must have the heart that says, "The trials I endure are gone because of you, and the trials I must face are gone because of you." Only then can we forget the historical sadness at that place and overcome the current sadness regarding individuals. When we consider that becoming such a person is God's deep intention, it becomes a question of when the members of the Unification Church, who follow God's will, have stood in such a position to worry about God.

When I have sadness, my prayer today is, "Father, please stop my sadness. Let sadness be Yours, and grant me only joy." Or, "Please remove our misfortunes and grant us blessings. If there are misfortunes, let them be Yours, and give me the blessings You have." This kind of faith will inevitably lead to failure. Such a person will not be able to walk the path of faith for long.

When you reflect on your personal history, if you discover that you have overcome difficult paths, you must recognize that God endured well before you overcame. Before rejoicing over the path you have walked, you must understand how much God has suffered. Consider God's position as He looks after and protects 3 billion people. If there is a parent with ten children, those children want everything to be done according to their own wishes and desires. This is the reality of fallen humanity.

All 3 billion people have their own convictions and expect God to act according to their own beliefs. If there are a thousand people, they all want God to do what is good for them. Can God do all of this? No. How wonderful it would be if He could grant everything they desire! Even when granted, humans complain. That is why in the course of history, sorrow and sadness continuously intersect and emerge.

When there are good times, there are also sad times. A person who has walked the path of suffering for good throughout their life may not see joy in that lifetime, but they will certainly see joy in the next generation. This is the path the Unification Church is on today. According to this principle, what path will the Unification Church take? What path will the leader of the Unification Church, Reverend Moon, take? What command will God, who guides Reverend Moon, give? This is the issue. This path is not one that seeks joy. It is a path taken to truly feel sadness. The heartbreaking sadness one feels is known only to the person involved. That is why the Unification Church emphasizes a faith that empathizes. 

Why do we emphasize a faith that empathizes? It is because without knowing God's sadness, one cannot approach God. To be filial to parents, a child must fully understand their parents' sadness and become a being who can remove that sadness with a heart that goes beyond it. If one’s heart is not aligned with that of the parents, they cannot be a filial child.

Until the parents' will is established to a global standard, humanity exists as the descendants under the archangel's dominion. If there is someone to teach, restoration cannot happen. Therefore, you must understand that God has not taught the core path of the restoration providence until now.  
Among the leaders, there are those who play around, thinking, "Only the teacher needs to know." Such behavior is not God's way. If such people exist, they will not be able to move forward. In order for you to become any kind of leader centered on the teacher, you must work harder than the teacher. The issue is how much you pray more than the teacher and how much you have a heart centered on the teacher's will. As long as it does not go against the will, evil naturally submits before good.  
**Trials and Growth**  
If there is a son who honors his grandfather, and that son has a son, when the father honors the grandfather, the son knows that his father is honoring him. The father who is honoring wants his son to be a filial son as well. From the perspective of a father who has the crown of filial piety, he would not want a son who is less filial than himself. He would say, "I have honored you this way, but I hope you honor me several times more." Why? Because "My honor is within the national realm of today's environment, but you must stand in the global realm and become a more remarkable filial son than I, representing the global realm." This is the desire of the parents. Parents want their children to be more filial than themselves. If there is a child who is less filial than himself, he will rebuke him. That rebuke is the only method to give blessings to the child. There is nothing else.  
I have never thought of myself when coming forth to serve God. I have never asked, "Why does God make His beloved son suffer like this for fifty years?" Rather, I thought of God as the one I should sympathize with. Even when being dragged to the Seodaemun Police Station, even when I was imprisoned, I thought this way. From the very first step of walking the path of the will, I expressed gratitude, saying, "Thank you for allowing me to live." I have walked this path to leave behind the historical standard of indemnity that has carried the traditional thought of the Unification Church. This is something that no one can infringe upon. No one can infringe upon it except for God the Father.  
As you all know, until Seong-jin graduated from college, I, as Seong-jin's father, never had the chance to be a father. This is a miserable thing. However, the issue is not that I am the father of that boy. The issue is how many people can call me father before I speak. "If what I do is wrong, then take up arms against your father. I will not resent you." I have thought this way. As long as I do not go against the will, evil naturally submits before good.  
**Trials and Growth**  
Because the parents have fulfilled their responsibilities before Heaven and walked in an environment that reveres Heaven, even if there are elements of dissatisfaction or unforgettably woven grievances from the past, they cannot kneel down. I have never held my children and wished for anything. If you look closely, God loves our family. This is undeniable. You may not know, but I can certainly say that.  
You must understand how dramatically the history of the world has changed from the 1960s to the 1970s. How did we bring about historical changes that had not occurred over thousands of years? It is because of the Unification Church. This is undeniable. Although I may seem like an ordinary person, it is undeniable that I have an impact on the world. The Unification Church will develop even if there is only one person left. You must have this conviction.  
Looking ahead to 1971, I told you that even if it costs me my life, I must walk this path. The issue is whether you are truly living up to your oath. Every spring, you must reflect on your past once more. If you are a tree that can bear fruit, or a living tree, when spring comes, you will initiate the movement of resurrection on your own. Thus, without any interference, you will pave the environment of resurrection according to the continuous natural law. When the sun shines warmly and the earth has moisture during the spring season, the living things will resurrect. Additionally, the spring season is when everything you possess is fully revealed. This continues through summer and autumn... Nature circulates this way. We humans are the same.  
Just because the teacher commands does not mean you simply move. What will happen if the teacher dies? At that time, everyone will pack their bags and leave. The issue is you. I will continue on my path even without you. However, if I am gone, you will not be able to continue on your path. Your descendants will not be able to either. It will lead to ruin. You must clearly understand this.  
**Trials and Growth**  
Live centered on tradition  
As I look around the trees I have planted, I see that I need to tend to them. Some trees have been planted so close together that they are less than a meter apart. If you have planted trees, you must nurture them with all your heart. Do you know how much heartfelt effort I put into buying this land and how much I struggled to purchase the land in Yeouido? Has anyone among you ever asked the teacher about such matters? Everyone just tries to take from the teacher... If that continues, it will lead to ruin. Such people will not be left alone by God.  
I know that there are local leaders who go hungry today. I see in prayer that someone is going hungry. However, I do not speak about it. As the time draws near, I want to see who among us truly possesses the correct understanding of the Unification Church. Therefore, you must make a new resolution. It cannot be vague. The thought of the Unification Church is a glorious and traditional thought handed down from Heaven. Historically, many ancestors have risked their lives to fulfill the will, and that will has been handed down centered on Heaven. Even as history passes, its essence does not change. It must not change.  
The big issue is whether you, who live looking toward the future, will realize that will before your descendants or not. Therefore, even when you marry in the future, you must choose a spouse who can align with that tradition. When you have children, you must give birth to sons who can stand in that position. You must not give birth to children of traitors. In loving your spouse, you must pray before God and make a commitment based on that pledge. This applies to individuals, families, churches, nations, and the world... Therefore, working for the will has eternal value. If you have planted trees... those trees will last forever. They will last forever along with the destiny of the Unification Church.  
The effort put into securing the land in Yeouido will last forever. However, if it is done for personal gain, it will all be lost within a lifetime. Therefore, strive to pursue eternal value and leave behind a page that can exist forever. That is why you must take risks. Such risks may not be possible in a world centered on humanity, but if there is a foundation known by God, recognized by the times, and aligned with the will, it will be realized. You must understand this.  
Throughout the process of walking the path of the will, many people have denied me. From Pyongyang until now, I can count on my fingers those who swore before Heaven and then fell away. I know exactly what they are doing now. I know who made such pledges in the past and what they are doing now.  
Among those present, if there are leaders or those who think they are doing well and justify their lives while criticizing others, what will happen to such people? Where will they bear fruit? The issue is bearing fruit.  
You must go through a path of suffering that is more miserable than that of enemies. You must extract the most precious seed from among many seeds. That one seed represents history. It is a victorious standard representing the times. It is not a standard seed of humanity but a standard seed of the heavenly kingdom. This kind of thought is necessary. The Unification thought is not a thought of being indebted.  
I have never thought of myself as your master. If you have a purpose that you can carry forward with your own conviction, leaving behind an eternal light, that purpose will remain even if you die. The loyalty to the will does not change. That integrity is bound to your life, so if you hold onto that integrity, you cannot be stopped wherever you go. With such conviction, you will also go to Heaven. You must understand that this kind of conviction is precious.  
**Trials and Growth**  
Blessings are good, but you must pay the price of suffering  
In spring, if you just sit still, you will not taste spring, but if you move around, the spring breeze will blow from all directions. The spring breeze is very fierce. However, it is here that life resurrects, and it is here that the movement of life occurs. You must think that if you overcome difficulties centered on these conditions, you will meet the ripe summer days.  
Therefore, you must first become a person like the unchanging seed. The heart of God, who created Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden, must pierce your heart. As those who have inherited the traces of the fall, we must rise above these traces, even if we bear resentment. Until now, the struggle to shed the traces of the fall has been the path of restoration history. This is the mission of the Unification Church in today's historical context, so those of us standing in this mission must align with the standard of that nature. Thus, it must become a perfect center that serves as a standard in any era. It must be undeniable. It must also be undeniable in the future. It must be real. Being real does not mean changing with external environmental changes. If you do not do this, you should not claim to walk the path of the will in the future.  
What I hope for you is to observe what the teacher is doing. The teacher does not live in debt. Organizations that operate in debt do not develop. The more you encounter trials, the more you must overcome them, and that becomes fertilizer. You must understand that this will become the compost pile for the future.  
You must be able to take root in that compost pile and grow. You must think about how you will develop in the environment and all conditions that allow you to grow well as you welcome spring. Thus, unless you solidify your position as an unchanging subject that can align with the original state at the time of creation and the state found today, your place will be broken. If the Unification Church cannot become such a group, it will stagnate.  
As I mentioned this morning, until now, the Unification Principle has only taught the content of individual indemnity. It has not taught the content of indemnity as a family. However, you must not forget this. Once you overcome the path of individual trials, the path of family trials begins from that point. Is the blessed family good? Blessings are good. However, along with the good, you must pay the corresponding price of suffering. You must sacrifice for the nation.  
Now, when we talk about enemies, those enemies are not personal enemies but family enemies, and the organization centered on the family is the enemy. The Unification Church can also become an enemy. If the Unification Church does not fulfill its loyalty to the Republic of Korea, it becomes an enemy. When the time comes, the environment of the Unification Church for good will grow into a global environment, and there will come a time when that environment will be settled all at once. You must understand that the spiritual world is being mobilized for that purpose.  
From this perspective, when you dissect your essence, the question always remains whether you can become a self that aligns with the content of that nature, which possesses the traditional thought of the Unification Church, where flowers bloom in spring and flourish in summer. The question is whether you can bear abundant fruit in autumn. You must become such people. The teacher will not live for a thousand years. Isn't that right? I will definitely leave a place for future generations. Those who inherit such a place will receive blessings beyond anyone else. Therefore, the path of receiving blessings must not be without value.  
Sometimes I reverse personnel appointments at the headquarters. You can learn about someone by placing them in reverse. It is to make them face difficulties. God trains in such a way. I have received such training a lot. That is why you must learn to discern these things. You must feel this once again.  
**Parents who honor their children want children who honor them even more**  
Now, in the remaining time today, we will plant trees. We must plant these trees with all our heart. When these trees grow, your descendants will come to the mountains in the future and rejoice at seeing these trees. I plan to build a university here in the future. I will create an educational institution. Therefore, you must plant trees on this land with great care. Even if I establish myself elsewhere in the future, I am thinking of either moving these trees or planting seeds here. In that sense, the land we have is the foundation that can love the internal stories that can save and protect history. Centered on Cheongpadae, we will...
To go through the passage of time and the environment, I bought this land here and also the land in Cheongpyeong.  
When viewed from the perspective of the headquarters, we need to buy a house where the teacher can reside. If we do that, there will be development in front of you. It is also good for the families. However, I cannot buy my house first due to my conscience. I must first establish the principle of building a heavenly temple that is hundreds or thousands of times larger than my house, and after making that promise, I can build my house.  
To do this, I have evangelized people who came to the Unification Church. I have devoted my utmost sincerity for those who have dedicated their youth and endured hardships for the purpose. No one understands why it must be done that way. I have fulfilled my responsibility towards the 36 families. I have done everything even while going into debt. Now I must establish my living situation. This is not for my comfort. It is for the dignity of the Unification Church. When outsiders come and see, the current state does not uphold the dignity of the Unification Church, so I do this to establish that dignity. It is also to establish the dignity of heaven. Therefore, you must have strength.  
The same goes for the headquarters of the association. To carry out planned projects, the headquarters must set a budget. Looking at the country, the government first decides the budget for the Blue House. Then, for each department, the budget is set according to the importance of each department. In the Unification Church, we must first set the budget centered around the teacher's family. If the association tries to look after its own living issues, it cannot do so with a clear conscience. Heaven does not help at all in that case. If that happens, it will lead to failure. No matter how well you live in the blue-roofed house, it is useless. Therefore, you must allocate a budget so that the teacher does not have to worry about living. Then God will resolve your living issues. However, the teacher does not even know whether he is eating or starving.... There is an order to thinking. However, such traditional standards are not established in the present. You must leave such traditional standards.  
It is done by establishing principles. The teacher does not want to be a dictator. It is because you must be better than me. You must put in more sincerity than I do. You must love the Father more than I do. Then I will be able to hand everything over to you. If there is a parent who is dutiful, that parent will wish for a child who is even more dutiful. Only then can a grandfather close his eyes and die when he passes away, and the father can also close his eyes and die when he passes away. The heart that can make the son endure more hardship than himself is loving the son. That is a natural thought. Thus, we must comfort God, who has worked hard alongside me. Because such sons and daughters are needed, and such successors are needed, we must carry out dutifulness that cannot be forgotten even in death, making them endure more hardship than I do. The teacher is stingy for my sake. He is someone who does not know how to spend money for my sake. He is not someone who goes into a restaurant and buys a meal for himself when he is hungry. He even interferes with what his mother eats and wears.  
A person must leave behind a motive. When the heart is thirsty, one must leave behind something that can make heaven shed tears. The descendants of such a person will not perish. Otherwise, no matter how loyal one is, they will fall out of favor. This is the teacher's philosophy of life. You must understand that this is a lesson taught by God and a truth inherited from Him.  
Work for the future  
I went in and out of the Unification Mountain every day. For 14 years, I crossed this Mangwuri pass every day. It was not for leisure. It may be said that it is the teacher's habit, but it is because I have made a promise before heaven. "Father, I swear before you to lay this foundation, so until that day, whether it rains or snows, I will come and go every day." If it is loyalty, I will not lose to anyone in the world. I do not lose to anyone in sincerity. If I am in such a position, I will not fail even in a place where I could fail. The same goes for you. Even if there are many hardships centered around the Unification Church, I am doing this while going into debt for that reason. I know that money is precious. Yet, I invest money equivalent to 50 million won.  
To inherit the traditional thought of loving the nation and people, we must build bridges. When building bridges, we must work at night and during the day when we are busy. These days, young people seem pathetic to me. It is wrong. They are foolish. When thinking about what kind of trials await us in the future and what the destiny of this nation is, today's misery is not the problem. Therefore, do not be someone who works for the present. While planting this tree today, think that way. Do not be someone who is happy receiving the rewards of today's hard work, but be someone who works for the future. Then you will not perish.  
If I were to pack my bags and leave, there would be a revival in the Unification Church across the country. I am someone who has that confidence. But why am I not appearing? I held the first, second, and third professors' meetings, and they say that the Unification Church's Teacher Moon is a successful person. Also, when I met a university president and had a private conversation, he said, "Teacher Moon of the Unification Church has now succeeded." He asked, "Why are you not appearing when you are doing great things?" It is not that I do not appear because I do not know that. I have experienced all of that in my youth.  
As the time approaches, the deeper the purpose is, the more it must confront one-on-one. If there is even one thing that gets caught up with the teacher, it is not just one person who is indemnified, but three generations are involved, and descendants are caught up as well. That is why the teacher did not say that he is the leader of the Unification Church even when he was in prison. Even if he has the ability to criticize their hearts, he did not do so. He thought about how to cultivate the way while being in a sorrowful position.  
Only those who remain loyal without change will survive.  
To fulfill the mission of restoring the archangel, you must work by putting yourselves forward. If you are loyal, your children will be loyal in the future. This tremendous fortune of restoration is connected to you. You must be sure not to forget this. This is not just for one generation but for several generations. Those who do not know this are miserable people. As I mentioned on the first day of April, April, May, June, July, and August are periods of trial. If there is no external persecution, internal trials arise. Therefore, you must become one with the wives who are on the front lines. You must also become one with the path of the purpose. When there is judgment internally, even God cannot handle it. It happens without anyone knowing, including outsiders. That is why only the humble will remain, and those who are loyal to the purpose will survive.  
You, who are heading towards the year 1971, must lay the foundation for normal and traditional Unification thought on the path of advancement. You must become a person who can align with your nature and transcend the world. You must be someone who does not lose to anyone in the world and can take pride on behalf of heaven. No matter how ruthless the times are and how painful the environment is, as long as you do not fall in that environment but can overcome the turning point of that environment, your path will be smooth.  
No matter how miserable it has been until now, your descendants will be able to go much easier than you, and you must make the year 1971 a year that remains in your life.  
A person in charge must not go into debt. The teacher is always a busy person. If he is tired, he is always tired. He is someone who lives with a sorrow that no one knows. You do not know well. Now, in the year 1971, you must think of a broader tomorrow and align with the path the teacher is taking. If you become one, you will prosper; if you do not become one, you will perish.  
You must understand that it is no longer centered on Korea. I told the Japanese association president, Kuboki, "As I go around this time, prepare this and that." I spoke about things I did not tell you. You should feel ashamed about that. The fact that I spoke to foreign members about things I could not say in front of the Korean Unification Church members means that you have not upheld the dignity of the host country. However, from now on, by establishing the condition of moving according to the teacher's orders and keeping that, you can uphold the dignity of the host country and establish your own dignity, and you must not forget that.  
Today, the position you are in as members of the Unification Church is not truly the position of Unification Church members. You must realize that there are still several passes we need to cross. You must understand that you must fight to fulfill God's will until the day you die. You must think again that you should have an unchanging purpose that can develop infinitely according to the source of unchanging nature, and I hope that you will spend the year 1971 and the 1970s meaningfully.  
Suffering and the Worth of Life  
We know that there are many changes in a person's life. We all know that we go through childhood, youth, and adulthood and reach old age. Here, I especially want to tell the young people that youth does not last long. And to the older people, I want to say that now that you are over 60 and approaching 70, or even nearing 100, you must go the path you need to go, but you cannot just go. You must leave behind a successor.  
How will you spend the peak of your life, your youth?  
Among the successors, there may be your grandchildren or great-grandchildren. If you do not leave behind someone among those successors who can take your place during your youth, it may be somewhat difficult to go the path you need to go. When you close your eyes and go to heaven, if you do not leave behind a young person who can work in your place in this world, that is, someone you can ask to fulfill the tasks you could not complete before the purpose, your path will not be smooth. Considering this issue, older people must strive to place their descendants before the purpose.  
April 18, 1971, (Sun), Unification Mountain.  
* This message was given after the Easter commemorative joint outdoor worship and tree planting event in Seoul, and the title was added by the editor.  
Next, young people must understand that their youth does not last long. Since they have already come to know the purpose, if they dedicate their precious youth completely to heaven without any regrets, how precious would that be?  
I sometimes see people who regret having spent their youth meaninglessly with the purpose, and those people are complaining and lamenting from a place where they have forgotten how valuable it is to have spent their youth with the purpose. There must be a peak during this youth. When looking at the youth period, from 20 years old to about 35 years old, there must be a peak during that time.  
Everyone has a peak period that can be called the best youth, and the question is who you spend that time with. Will you spend it with your father and mother, with a purpose-driven teacher, with your family, or will you immerse yourself in your work or school centered around yourself? When considering these things, what is the most valuable way to spend that time? Is it not more precious to spend it for the happiness of the nation or the world, rather than for your own happiness or the happiness of your family, in a way that can remain forever in history? Even when we think universally, we cannot help but think that way.  
So how should we spend that time? When you understand that this purpose is a heavenly purpose, the question becomes what kind of attitude you will have while surpassing the peak of youth centered around this purpose. In other words, how will I feel happiness before the purpose, and will I live on a foundation of hope to advance toward a better happiness centered around the purpose? Will I live in the most lonely position, opposing numerous nations and peoples, even if I become a sacrifice for the world, and value that?  
When you think of your youthful years, you may think of them as the happiest and best time. However, when viewed from the perspective of public purpose, it is happier to be remembered by God and to receive His sympathy, even if it is in a lonely position, than to be in an outwardly good environment. Even if you become a sacrifice among numerous people and sovereigns, that position can be a good opportunity to illuminate your youth, and we must understand that.  
Living through the process of twists and turns is also a worthwhile endeavor.  
Greater happiness does not begin from the joy of a day but starts from the time of glory that can bloom amid the trials of thousands and millions of years. In such a position, a higher-dimensional foundation of happiness sprouts, and through such connections, that happiness appears on earth. When we think of this, it seems that living a meaningful life through the process of twists and turns is a worthwhile life as a human being.  
When we look at nature, we see that various trees and grasses have different shapes. When we see a well-grown tree, we might think that it grew comfortably, but that tree must have worked hard behind the scenes to absorb the nutrients that suit its qualities. There may also be trees that, while absorbing the necessary nutrients for growth, suffer from various opposing forces and undergo a process of struggle. When we see such trees, their outward appearance may be twisted and shriveled. However, when we humans look at a well-grown tree, we can evaluate it externally, but when we look at a poorly grown tree, we tend to feel sympathy for it.
The twisted and contorted tree carries a history of hardships that no other tree behind it possesses. It stands in a path of suffering, perhaps because there is a rock beneath its roots, or it is planted on a rock and must root itself in the crevices, unable to stretch out otherwise. This is why it grows in such a twisted manner. People generally desire trees that grow smoothly and upright, but such trees have a much shorter experience than those that grow in a twisted way. The characteristic of a twisted tree is its strength. Although it may not be tall, shriveled, and thin, each segment of this tree is strong.

When a freely grown tree segment collides with a segment grown through trials, which one will break? A segment that grew without undergoing suffering will break, while a segment that overcame difficult conditions during its growth will not break. It is not only the large that is good; while large may be good, a tree that has grown through trials is strong. The strong endure.

What happens if a tree grows well up to a certain point but encounters a rock that hinders its roots from spreading? That tree will die there. If a rock lies beneath the roots that have grown normally up to that point, no matter how hard the tree tries to break through the rock, it will inevitably die because it cannot penetrate the rock from its current position.

However, a twisted tree that grows by pushing its roots through the crevices of the rock will extend infinitely if there is fertile soil beneath the rock. This tree possesses the life force to break through the rock, even if it encounters it while extending infinitely. But you must understand that a tree that grows smoothly and looks good on the outside will find it extremely difficult to sustain itself when the environment changes drastically.

From a perspective of purpose, the path of restoration does not mean a smooth road. The path of restoration must necessarily go through the path of indemnity and return. Only after going through the path of indemnity and return does the normal path of restoration unfold before us, and we must understand that the moment this normal path of restoration ends is when the time of glory arrives.

The path of indemnity and return is a path of suffering. It requires us to root ourselves in an environment where no one rejoices, paying the price of sacrifice and blood, and to leave behind the life force. This is the path of indemnity and return. 

If we speak of a tree, it is akin to a pine tree that begins to root itself in the crevices of a rock. Other trees around may be happy to have a good foundation to grow, but the pine tree rooted in the rock's crevice faces a very dangerous environment where its survival is at stake as the rock heats up more in the sunlight. If this tree survives and grows for one year, two years, three years without dying, then even if greater trials come before it, it can survive, but a tree that has not endured such trials will break when faced with hardship.

In this perspective, isn't the historical process that humanity has undergone similar? If God, who aims for goodness and true meaning, seeks true human seeds, what kind of seeds will He seek? Will He seek seeds from a nation that has grown smoothly and well, like the American people today, who have formed a global cultural sphere in a short historical process, a nation that anyone can admire? If He sought seeds from a nation enjoying the best culture within the current civilization, while it may develop beyond that lifestyle, if there is a path that stands in opposition to providence, wouldn't it all fall back?

Considering this, God's restoration providence does not unfold through a smooth path but rather involves a historical process that must go through a path of suffering. God seeks seeds of people who, although shriveled and seemingly weak, possess the life force to absorb nutrients and remain in the historical process.

If there is a being that overcomes difficulties on the path of trials and strengthens its own life force, then even when greater trials come upon it, it will have the resolution to break through and fight. However, those who have grown naturally will panic and retreat when faced with several times the trials.

In light of this, God works through a persevering nation in history. Not only a persevering nation but also a race or nation that possesses the life force to overcome all kinds of suffering in an environment where no one can remain, especially at the final critical juncture of storms. To fulfill the providential path that must overcome the final global suffering, it must be a group or nation that possesses the mindset to be grateful even if it means exchanging its life.

When we consider this issue, such a group or nation will surely remain in history. An example of a nation with such a mindset is the Israeli people, who, since the day they persecuted Jesus 2,000 years ago, have become a nation that roams the world, having been forsaken by God. However, with a mindset of revering God and believing themselves to be the chosen people, they possess a thorough ideological origin that no environmental conditions can uproot. As they navigate the flow of history, even if they encounter crossroads of death, they center themselves on their national pride and stand before God, swearing allegiance and holding onto Him. 

Because they are a chosen people born from such historical connections, God cannot destroy the will of the Israeli people, and it is certain that this nation will usher in a new era capable of leading the world.

Therefore, when we look at the Israeli people today, there is no place they have not been. They are everywhere. Those who hold authority in the global academic field are among the Jewish people. No matter how wealthy a nation America may be today, it is the Jewish people who hold two-thirds of the wealth. The financial power of Wall Street is controlled by the Jewish people. This is also true in the political sphere and in all other fields. In the Soviet Union, more than one-third of the top officials are Jewish.

Considering these facts, how can a nation that has suffered become a significant force in the world, bearing important responsibilities and standing in a position that other nations cannot attain? This suggests that God wishes to restore the world through such a persevering nation. When this nation overcomes all trials and establishes its sovereignty to achieve global victory, how great will that joy be? That joy will indeed be a historical joy.

All the tyrants and evil political ideologies that opposed them over thousands of years will not remain as mockery of this nation's glorious day when it achieves victory, but rather become a motive that can stimulate the value of global and cosmic glory.

The more one has walked the path of suffering, the better they understand God's will. Those who feel the worth of their suffering treat that suffering's purpose with greater respect. When viewed through the lens of God's will, those who walk the path of suffering with their lives at stake will understand its value better than anyone else. If such individuals come together to form a nation, that nation will understand the value of God's will more deeply and widely than any other nation.

Thus, when it comes to following the path of purpose or practicing the principles of heavenly fortune, it is better to face trials than to seek happiness. Trials are God's strategy to ensure that our descendants do not perish. If we inherit traditions built on sacrifice and trials and develop further, we will be able to break through any difficult path in the future. However, a nation that has not laid this foundation will face despair when it encounters difficulties after having celebrated a glorious day.

This is why God's will stands on the position of developing through the intensified path of indemnity. 

When individuals are restored, the restoration of families remains, followed by the restoration of tribes, nations, states, the world, and the cosmos, with multiplied and intensified paths of suffering ahead. God, who knows this, gives trials to those who can walk this path and follow His will. Those who reject this cannot receive greater blessings. If you wish to receive blessings beyond life, you can, but if you desire blessings below life, you will only receive blessings below that level.

Today, the question is where we can find the subjective power to resurrect humanity, which is under the dominion of death, into the realm of life. Therefore, even if it means paying the price of sacrifice greater than life, if there is a nation that understands that greater value and can confidently break through to establish it, the more it walks the path of suffering, the more it will not perish but will lay a foundation that possesses a life force that is stronger, thicker, and more upright than anything else.

The path that the Unification Church is taking is also one that is equipped to go this way. You must understand that this is the main thought of the teacher who has been guiding the path of indemnity and restoration until now. Unification Church members should embrace this thought. They should not become people who criticize themselves while looking sideways. We must go on and on.

Before any subject speaks, they should encourage and stimulate each other to move forward. Even if the one giving such orders is an old man, even if he is a wrinkled elder rather than a young person boasting a beautiful smile, we must listen to him. Even if he is an old man with white hair blowing in the wind, if a single word of resolution from that old man has the power to judge the youth, you must understand that God weaves the motives for the development of heavenly history around the old man who has aged and shriveled.

Young people must respect the elderly. Today, even the so-called leaders of the Unification Church have the mindset that they cannot take responsibility unless it is them, but such a decadent mindset should not exist. Do not think that God cannot work through you. The older people put in more sincerity than you do. They have only one path to walk. They have no horizontal hopes. You must understand this.

Young people may be filled with the bundles of desires that spread horizontally, but those over sixty years old, as their white hair increases year by year, have only one thing left to prepare for their final destination. This is their destiny. Therefore, they love the will more than anyone else to fulfill it, and they stand in a position to advance tirelessly toward a single purpose to establish themselves as the most fulfilling beings before that will, but young people do not do this. Rather, young people are filled with fantasies and delusions. 

From this perspective, young people must understand that the older generation has the potential to leave expectations for God and that God can place His hopes in them. Young people should not disregard the elderly. Although an elderly person may come with a wrinkled face, they should not be dismissed. Even if they have lost their teeth and have gold caps, just looking at their mouth may make one feel uncomfortable. Their face may be wrinkled, with no taut areas, and their body may seem frail, as if it could blow away with a gust of wind, but you must fear such grandmothers. A single word from this grandmother is not just a personal thought; it conveys a purpose through the spirit world. 

This is connected to their ancestors and is an important link in supporting the lives of the martyrs of Christian history. Young people should not try to solve their difficulties alone when they encounter hardships. When faced with difficulties, they should consult their grandmothers or report to their fathers. A wise person does this. No matter how large the surface roots are, if there is no motivation for the original root to be large, the outer roots cannot spread strongly.

This is why we must not stand in a position to disregard such grandmothers. However, today in the Unification Church, there are many who criticize those who pray. This is a current problem within the Unification Church. The teacher has seen many irresponsible actions in the world of faith. The teacher himself calls such grandmothers to ask what they have said in the spirit world. Although the teacher knows everything, the grandmothers speak through the spirit world. 

When followers of the teacher say such things, does the teacher not know? He does not speak. He calls them to talk with those who do not believe. People need stimulation. No matter how much one knows, that knowledge alone does not provide stimulation. No matter how much one knows, it is through distributing that knowledge through someone less capable that the stimulation comes alive. This is the principle of creation.

When the subject and the object interact, reproduction occurs. No matter how perfect the subject is, it cannot stand alone. There must be relative conditions for reproduction to occur. This is the principle of creation. Therefore, to present this, such grandmothers are absolutely necessary. Even if you feed them, you must take care of such grandmothers.

From this perspective, today’s leaders may wish to take a cute girl as their wife and live with her, but those who wish to honor such grandmothers as spiritual parents and ancestors, and who want to be more dutiful than their own children, are rare.

When we look at the history of restoration today, the history of restoration must revive the past in the present and indemnify it. Therefore, you yourselves must reflect on the past.
The heart that can love one's historical ancestors must develop internally, and you must understand that without respecting those older than yourself in reality, you cannot achieve the conditions for restoration and resurrection. If there are older people or those who are struggling on the path of faith, I hope that young people will raise their hands if they have ever tried to serve them for even just one month, like their own mother or grandmother. Without such ideological content, if one focuses only on oneself and desires only for one's own success, that person will fail. The path of only wanting to do well for oneself cannot become a good. Wanting only for oneself stands in a position that denies the whole and thus cannot receive support. When we see that we can clearly understand this through the relationships of life that occur around our daily lives, it is the same with God.

To become a central being that leaves heavenly blessings on this earth, one must walk the path of suffering for God's will and love those who have suffered throughout their lives even more than their own future sons and daughters. When you think about this fact, you should understand how blessed it is to serve those who have worked hard in the past rather than those who will work hard in the future.

Going out with Jesus is the same position. If Jesus were alive today, He would be 2,000 years old. Do not think He died at 33 years old. What kind of grandfather would He have become at 2,000 years old? Have you thought about that? Does a filial child have to make their parents able to be filial? Does a loyal subject become loyal only when the king shows them the way? Today, Christians love the young Jesus, but what if Jesus were bent, thin, and bald? Would you still follow Him? There are those who give advice when things are good and those who congratulate when things are good. Who is the true person?

April 25, 1971 (Sunday) Early morning, Headquarters Church.

We walk the daily path of life, not knowing when or what suffering we may encounter, so you must protect us. While it is important for us to walk our own path amidst the flowing history, we must also clearly understand the tremendous responsibility we bear in fulfilling our duty of filial piety and loyalty before you.

The world may try to pull me along, but my heart is led by you, Father. When I discover myself caught in between, I realize that to take even one more step toward you, I must commit to my daily life. Please allow us to understand that we must have such a commitment to become that kind of person.

The steps we have taken to come to the Unification Sanctuary are not merely steps to affirm our personal victory; we carry the responsibility to save not only individuals but also families, and beyond families, to save tribes, nations, and the world. We are on a path of destiny that we must confront centered on ourselves, so your infinite love must be poured out even more upon us. They must clearly understand that this is essential. We were not born for anyone else. We were born for you, Father, and we must realize that we were born with the mission to eliminate the evils of the world.
