When we think of this, today is not a moment for ourselves. Today must not be a life centered on ourselves.

Father, please guard the path we must take. We know that you have worked hard to bestow a mission upon this nation and people, and we must also understand that the steps of that effort must not be in vain. You must protect this nation. Centered on this nation, we are to decide a precious responsibility in the near future, so please raise up your beloved ones who can align this nation with your will, who will obey and serve you, and allow them to lead this nation as children who are trusted by you from the place of glory.

Considering that Asia will face difficult positions in the future, you must personally lead this nation. More than anyone else, we must be concerned for this nation, and we must unite to firmly embrace the path this people must take, paving the way to align with your will. Whenever we think of this, we realize that we are in a busy position. We feel how heavy the responsibility is to fight and win. We know well that we must start for the sake of justice, so may we follow the footsteps of you, the center of justice, and emulate your unwavering integrity toward the goal of goodness, fighting until the end, and may we be your children who do not neglect our duties in fulfilling our purpose.

On this day, please be with the countless children who gather here, focusing their hearts and bowing before your will. You know well where they should go, where they should stay, and what they need to prepare, so please manifest your will over all who move with understanding, and let the bond of love be the foundation. Please personally oversee that foundation so that it can become a starting point that spreads out as a stepping stone to victory on this earth.

Please be present with the beloved children who are fighting for your will in every field. Moreover, weak women are stepping forward to fulfill this era's mission, standing in positions that no one can imagine, embracing heaven and shedding tears. If they feel sorrow from all the environments surrounding them, please comfort them a thousandfold, ten thousandfold, and help them to carve out a path to victory. Let this journey be one that fulfills your will, knowing that it is indeed the path required by this era. We earnestly ask and desire that this period becomes a precious time to overcome the history of sorrow and tears that has been shameful before heaven.

Please allow today to be a proud day before you. We earnestly hope that you will be with us in every place where we gather today. We entrust all that will happen in the future to you, and we earnestly hope that you will personally oversee this time, as we offer all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> We know well that humanity is seeking to find the world of lost hope again. Since the day when the ancestors of humanity betrayed God's will in the Garden of Eden and fell, humanity has fallen into a place of sorrow. However, the question is whether that sorrow is the degree of sorrow you feel in your life or whether it is something greater than that.

When a person who is deeply immersed in despair feels the pain of sorrow acutely and breaks free from that despair, they can gain a new sense of hope. Considering that we must transition from the realm of sorrow to the realm of hope, we must understand that this sorrow is not limited to one's individual self.

Sorrow transcends oneself; it relates to a beloved wife if one has one, to children if one has them, that is, it is centered around family, and it is also connected to one's relatives, or to the nation and the world, and furthermore, we know that all of history up to now has flowed from this sorrow. This sorrow did not begin with me but is rooted in the sorrow inherited from our ancestors, flowing throughout all of history. When we think of this fact, we must realize that the sorrow I experience does not end with me but is connected to historical content.

What is the source of this sorrow? What is the root of sorrow? It is this sorrow that connects to suffering, and this sorrow serves as a motive that can lead us today to a place of despair, to a place of defeat, and even to a place of death. You are seeing and feeling far too many sad realities around you compared to joyful events. Without breaking free from such a sorrowful environment, the world of joy we desire, the paradise of joy, will not come.

So, when we seek to reach the world of joy and the paradise of joy, can we get there with our own strength? We cannot escape from a sorrowful place with our own limited strength. That is why faith is necessary here. The more we feel sorrow, the more we need the source of strength that can alleviate and minimize that sorrow in proportion to the depth of our feelings. When we realize that we are surrounded by the realm of sorrow and that we cannot overcome or conquer that sorrow on our own, we come to require a center that can overcome it, that is, we need some kind of entity. That is what faith is, and you must understand this.

Thus, a person of faith must not be dragged along by the sorrowful place, but must be equipped to prevent becoming a sorrowful place, to eliminate sorrowful factors, and to push forward. Only those who live with such a personal environment can be called people of faith. Furthermore, when we consider the posture of a person of faith, we must not remain limited to our individual positions but must be able to connect it to a global dimension. In our terms, it must be universal.

Today’s humanity must traverse this vast universal path, and it is the path that must be taken in life, a path of destiny from which we cannot escape. However, one cannot walk that path with a mindset that one is planning and going alone. Therefore, we must go with the will of the one who is the object of our faith and the center of our faith, that is, we must abandon our own will and center ourselves on His will, abandon our own purpose and center ourselves on His purpose. In other words, the question is how to return from the purpose of sorrow and the position of a sorrowful self to the purpose of joy and to a self that can rejoice.

No matter how much a person resolves to do something, we know that such resolutions do not last a year. We have often seen and experienced that the plans made on the first day of the lunar new year change within a few months. From this perspective, even if I have resolved to do good, as someone included in the realm of fallen rights and death, that resolution cannot escape the realm of sorrow.

From this standpoint, the question of how I can have hope or resolution that can break through this realm of sorrow, or how I can have a conscious determination while living here, is crucial. The question is how to secure a self that can claim to be within a realm of goodness that transcends this world of death. This will determine whether we can dispel the current sorrowful environment and occupy the realm of goodness. You must understand this fact.

Even if one has already made that determination, even if one has already become aware of it and resolved to do so, that resolution is only temporary and not lasting. When we consider whether we can continue on that path for a year, ten years, or a lifetime, we feel this is a deeply hopeful issue through our life of faith. No matter how much one resolves, one cannot achieve that resolution alone.

Since we are already captured within the realm of death from the fall, we are beings who cannot overcome it alone, who cannot walk that path alone. No matter how much we struggle to rise, we are beings who will fall back down, and thus we cannot escape the realm of sorrow, nor can we transcend that limit. When we consider this issue, we must understand that no matter how much effort we put in, if that effort starts from ourselves, it will ultimately lead back to ourselves.

That is why we must have the belief that it is not by starting from ourselves but by transcending through the Absolute, through the absolute faith, that this beginning is possible. This is the issue. With this belief, I know that God is present as I walk that path. I also know that there is Satan, who stands in opposition to God. And I understand that within my sphere of life, good and evil are intertwined.

Therefore, when we stand on the side of evil amidst this intertwining of good and evil, it brings sorrow, and when we stand on the side of good, it brings joy. When we align with Satan, sorrow intensifies, and when we align with God, joy begins. Considering this issue, when a believer has absolute faith centered on God and prioritizes good, a way to transcend the world of sorrow will be sought.

And when we start centered on good and on God, the question of how much difference there is between our past and today will determine whether we can advance or retreat. When today possesses content that can develop further than yesterday, we will take a step forward into the realm of goodness, and we will advance further toward God. However, if today becomes stagnant compared to yesterday, we will find ourselves in a position contrary to goodness.

If I have established an absolute relationship centered on good, the sorrow of the good world will be lifted. My own sorrow can inflict sorrow on the good world, and the sorrow of a fallen individual can bring about God's sorrow.
is something that can weigh heavily upon us. Therefore, standing in such an immense position is what makes us human, and it is this journey of faith that we are striving towards. My personal sorrow does not end with just my own grief; it adds sorrow to the good world and makes the heavenly world, or God's heart, feel sorrow even more. All of this is determined by me.

When I find myself in such a state, or when I stand in a place of lamentation, regret, and despair on my faith journey, I am not the only one standing there. God, who is the center of faith and should not be in a place of sorrow, stands there, and the heavenly world stands there as well. Furthermore, the foundation of goodness that future good descendants must walk upon, as well as the historical foundation of goodness that ancestors who have come and gone throughout history fought for and achieved, all of that is also lamenting because of me.

Considering this fact, if I stand in such a place, then the good path for me will be that much further away, and God will also be that much further away. In that case, Satan will solidify his stage in proportion to that distance, and from that solid foundation, he will rise against me and attack before God. We must always feel that we are standing on such a battlefield.

Individuals must determine good and evil. We must stand in a position where we advocate for goodness, align ourselves with goodness, and become a motivating force for the advancement of goodness. However, we can also find ourselves in a position that stimulates evil in a negative sense, where evil stands against goodness and sacrifices it. This is influenced by my faith life. Therefore, you must not think that your current position is solely your own.

The question arises whether a single word I speak determines good or evil, or whether a single action determines good or evil. A single word, a single expression can determine whether something is good or evil, whether it can stimulate joy or sorrow within me. That sorrow and joy are not limited to me alone. They are related to this vast universe, this vast world, and this vast history.

When we think about the tremendous position of a believer, we must understand that in our journey of faith today, we cannot speak carelessly, act carelessly, or think carelessly. If a single word is spoken incorrectly, it establishes an absolute condition under which evil can acknowledge itself. It means that goodness cannot assert itself as goodness. No matter how much goodness tries to assert itself, it will inevitably have to concede to evil. In other words, although you as an individual may be very small, the entire universe is weighing itself based on you. The world of good and evil is in confrontation. The historical world of the past, present, and future is rising and falling based on you. You must feel this tremendous reality.

For example, when you encounter someone, such as your child or a friend, in a habitual manner, you may see them as the same person you knew in the past. However, God may have chosen that person as a representative to fulfill His purpose in the future, without you even knowing it. As long as you are unaware of this fact, you will treat that person habitually as you did in the past. If you approach that person with a habitual mindset and strike them from an evil standpoint, that strike can lead to the despair of hope in their path, causing God to fall into a position of lamentation. This is not simply an issue of individual habits but a historical issue that can rise and fall.

Therefore, even if a single word seems to have no content in everyday life, it can bring about certain results for the person who hears it. Even a seemingly insignificant expression can lead to certain results for the person who sees it. Your single word and expression carry historical significance. You must always remember that you stand in such a position.

When a person falls, it does not happen all at once. A momentary feeling, something that can be passed off as nothing, can become the origin of downfall. A word that seems insignificant can be the origin and starting point of tremendous evil. When you think about this, you realize that a single expression can determine the world of death and can become a marker for the complete stage of Satan to begin. We must always keep this fact in mind.

In this way, good and evil are not determined by a lifetime of struggles but can be decided in a moment. It is at the moment when you take a step, even while wavering, that a decision is made. Isn’t that right? Even a journey of a thousand miles begins with a single step, and a life of goodness also begins with careful steps.

It is not about turning around 180 degrees all at once but about making one step at a time. From this perspective, your position as a believer is like adjusting the balance of a scale. If the scale is even slightly off, it will tip back and forth. Isn’t this the position of today’s believer? Therefore, your expression can represent the path of goodness and can stand in for heaven and earth. You must recognize that you are in such a position.

First, you must recognize that God has labored for you. Therefore, what you must vow in your life is that if the right side is God’s side, you must seek God and go to the right side. Thus, you must rise to the right side. Going to the right side and rising up means moving from a position of sorrow to a position of joy. To those who knock, it will be opened, and this applies to everyone.

When you change direction, you are always consuming energy without realizing it. You must understand that without supporting this energy, you cannot endure your current position or establish a relationship with God. Even at this moment, the consumption of energy is intensifying. A fierce battle of energy consumption is ongoing.

So where will this consumed energy be replenished? First, I must replenish it myself. When I discover that I can replenish it myself, I can maintain my current state. Furthermore, God must reinforce my strength. However, if I receive God’s strength, it is not my merit. It is God’s merit.

If you have walked the path of purpose for ten years, it is not because of your own merit that you have done so. You must not forget that it is because of God’s labor and the foundation of His achievements that you have walked this path. Therefore, when you realize that you have remained before the purpose until now and that you are advancing toward tomorrow, you must have the heart that says, “I have placed too much burden on God and incurred too much debt.”

From this perspective, on the path of faith, the further you go, the less you should justify yourself. Instead of justifying yourself, you should deepen your repentance before God. You must elevate the virtue of humility that allows you to confess and bow your head before God. This is the attitude that a believer should have.

When I look back at my past, it is clear that I am a descendant of corruption. However, if I stand in a good position in the present, it is not because of my own excellence. It is because of the merits of my ancestors, and because God has paid the price of countless sufferings to leave a foundation for my life in the present.

For example, let’s say I am living now. I eat and live. However, regarding this fact of living, you have no relationship or thoughts about it. You only know that you are living. You think that physical fatigue can be restored after just one night’s sleep. But behind the fact that you are living, there is a fierce battle between death and life that continues.

Before you realize it, before you have the conviction that you are living, at the very bottom of your being, there is a fierce struggle over whether it is death or life. It is because you are defending against the line of death and standing in a position that has overcome the line of death that you are able to live. However, if you lose that foundation, there is a risk that the invasion of the realm of death will begin.

When you fall ill, you experience pain, but where does that pain come from? Isn’t that pain the tragedy of an individual that obeys the world of death? This is the issue. Although you live habitually in your daily life, you must always remember that you are standing in a place where you are maintaining life by having completely subdued death through a fierce struggle.

In your journey of faith, God is laboring at the very bottom, consuming infinite energy centered on goodness, even when you are unaware of it. It is under such compensation that you can experience joy today and can have the awareness that you stand before God or goodness. Without such rewards and without paying such a price, you cannot establish yourself.

Why is that? Because if your roots are in the realm of corruption today, you must stand in a position above your roots, or if it is religion, you must stand in a position above religion for change to occur.

You must always stand in a position of awareness. Considering this issue, although humans born from evil should bear fruit from evil, the fact that I can pursue goodness and long for God today is not because of myself but because of God. What belongs to God must be offered as God’s, and to create a foundation where we can smoothly exchange what belongs to God, we must risk our lives and align ourselves with that.

The results of such efforts do not begin with me but begin after I meet God. Therefore, even when I rejoice, I must rejoice after God has first rejoiced. This is the principle of the position of a believer who follows God. However, if there is joy, one might say, “This is my joy. I have done well, and that is why this joy has come to me; it is naturally my joy.” When one stands in a position to assert this fact, you must understand that another subject that is contrary to God arises from there.

Thus, you must always think that we are standing in a triangular zone. The position I am currently standing in is a triangular zone. When viewed from the center of my individual self, my heart and body are in a struggle between God and Satan. Therefore, if I contribute to God, I am going to God’s side, and if I go the opposite way, I am going to Satan’s side. Even if I bear great responsibility in my life, whether it is at the individual, family, or national level, it is a triangular operation based on national standards. In that context, if I take a step correctly, I become a national benefactor, but if I take a step incorrectly, I become a national enemy. I become a traitor.

So who makes that decision? It is not God. As we see in principle, it is the individual who makes it. Who makes the decision? I must bear this responsibility. The factors that can make that decision should not be taken lightly or lost at any time. They must always be in your heart. This is the highest target you must fight and win as a believer, and it will be the standard of victory.

When we forget this, the starting point and the result become different. If you are swept away from the starting point, you will naturally find yourself in a position that is negated in the present.

Therefore, you must have the awareness that God is always alive. Even if there is loneliness and you encounter difficult paths of suffering, you must not forget that heart. To meet joy at the highest place, you must die at the highest place.

In other words, when autumn comes, trees shed their leaves, and in winter, they store all their sap in their roots. Such trees do not die in winter and, in spring, sprout new life due to their roots. In the same way, as we walk the path of faith, the more difficult it becomes, the more we must concentrate a life motive within ourselves. If we lose that concentrated life motive, we cannot find it by being passive due to external factors. We must have the heart that says, “I cannot miss this,” from a proactive position in order to find it.

From this perspective, you must fight. If you have lived a life of faith for ten years, that ten years must have been a struggle to unite with God’s heart. And when you feel great joy in facing something, that stimulus must lead to a day when you can achieve it. Such thoughts must always remain deep within your heart. If you find yourself surrounded by difficult circumstances, you must have the conviction that “When spring comes, I will once again unleash this and reach to the ends of heaven. Just wait and see; when that time comes, I will go like this.”

Through difficult circumstances, we must gather materials. We must understand how evil is evil and its schemes, and measure how wide and extensive the range of evil is. We must gather strength that exceeds the power with which evil attacks goodness and prepare for greater offensive capabilities. There will come a time when we must fully invest. Even if you are caught in sorrow on your faith journey, if you cannot have the conviction that “This heart will be released at some point,” you cannot walk the path of faith.

Moreover, you must consider that we were born from evil, and thus we are inherently in harmony with evil. Therefore, if we do not always remain vigilant, discerning, and aligning ourselves with the standard of goodness, we will inevitably turn back to evil. Habitual paths...
because it cannot escape its origin, the result of our habitual path, which has its roots in evil, must inevitably be evil. Therefore, the life of a believer who does so is akin to taking a path opposite to the one they swear to follow. Thus, the opposing force there always manifests as a proportional action. We must eliminate the consumption caused by this proportional action and continue to live each day, each moment, rising to the right if it is right, and upward if it is upward. Otherwise, we will not be able to progress and develop towards the heavenly side. This is the problem.

The Reason God Gives Joy
Today, the Unification Church itself is like this. If you observe Unification Church members quietly, at one time they make a big fuss about working for a purpose. Who is that for? One must understand that good things have historical significance. One must also recognize that good things have a sense of the times. Additionally, it must be understood that they are related to the future. If you deny historical significance, you cannot be qualified to possess joy. If you stand in a position that denies the sense of the times, you cannot acknowledge that joy. If you stand in a position that denies the joy of having a future, then joy will not remain before you as you must go towards the future.

The joy you feel is the same in today's Unification Church. That joy is not God's will to determine a central point of an era from God's heart before creation, through the creation process, and up to the completion of restoration. It is also a joy to establish the origin of the future's starting point. Therefore, having this joy means representing history, representing the times, and representing the future.

Thus, joy should not be rooted in oneself. It must be planted in reality and a foundation for the future must be prepared. Therefore, we should rejoice with the world, rejoice with the future, and thus, the spirit world should also receive the resolution of grievances and rejoice. If that has become the origin, then it is the principle of the universe that such results should be borne.

If you think that you alone will rejoice, you will lose all that joy. The joy related to history will depart when history leaves you, and if the joy is related to the times, forgetting that historical connection will cause the environmental conditions of the times to take away that joy. The joy you possess should become the foundation for future joy, but if you do not have the origin of the future, that joy can shatter into pieces.

Without knowing the content, one may fuss about heaven and then later feel as if it was all a dream. If you quietly observe the spiritual history, it is the same. John the Baptist was like that. When Jesus was called the beloved son of God, he fervently testified, but when that heart left him, he stood in a position saying, "Isn't Jesus, who lived as a bastard, inferior to me in every way?"

For me, joy must not be a personal joy for oneself but a global joy. Therefore, the greater the joy, the more one must advance towards something higher, nobler, and more valuable than oneself. In today's fallen world, which is the foundation of evil and sorrow, if you have had a moment where you felt any joy and could gather the world's environment to reach a place beyond that joy, how precious would that be?

That is something that cannot be bought with a thousand or ten thousand pieces of gold, nor can it be bought with this era or the past. It is something that cannot be possessed without paying the price of the three eras: the past, present, and future. You must not consider the joy that God has given you in conjunction with you as your own. Is that yours? Those who think it is theirs will perish. That is what a thief does. What was given to you was given on behalf of history, what you felt was felt on behalf of history, and what placed you in that position was established by God to solidify the start of the future. Yet, do you think you can do as you please in such an environment?

The Correct Attitude a Believer Should Have
Therefore, the attitude of a believer must always be that of a debtor. You must understand this. What is the most important attitude as a believer? It is the attitude of a debtor. Have you ever been in debt? If you have nothing to owe, try to get into debt a little to experience it. Understand what it means to be a debtor. Stand in a position where you cannot repay a debt. It is truly miserable. If you owe even a penny, you can be grabbed by the collar, and fundamentally, your character can be denied. Isn't that so? There is no dignity there.

A debt must be repaid. When a creditor sees a debtor trying to repay their debt, they will feel sympathy. Isn't that right? However, if a debtor does not even dream of repaying their debt and instead spends money to buy good things and eat whatever they want, trying to live well for themselves, that becomes a source of trouble. Isn't that so? A debtor must always have the attitude of wanting to repay their debt. When the determination to repay the debt becomes greater than the debt itself, the creditor cannot accuse that person. Rather, they will feel sympathy for them. Isn't that so?

The attitude of a believer must be like that of a debtor. When some joy or benefit comes to oneself, to whom should it be returned? At that time, one must have the heart to repay the debt. If something joyful happens to oneself, one should think that they must repay the debt centered around that joy. You must not claim it as yours. If a debtor is urged by the creditor and does not respond, they are completely denied. Therefore, one must not think that joy can arise because of oneself.

When observing the leaders of the Unification Church, some people do not appreciate the principle lectures they receive and feel bad about it; such people are not qualified to be leaders. Those who judge based on themselves are failures. Even when Chairman Yoo was around, if someone criticized him for being responsible for something, the question is whether that person did well as a leader. Do they treat their children well when they go home? Do they treat their friends well? Those who occupy the position of heavenly justice and then complain about this and that are Satan. Such people are direct subordinates of Satan. Those who sit idly and criticize are Satan. So, did you fulfill your responsibilities while making those comments?

A filial child does not become one just by treating their parents well. A filial child must also treat their children well. They must teach their children the right path. To be a filial child, they must also make their grandchildren filial to their grandparents. If a grandchild becomes a delinquent, can a son say to his parents, "My child is bad, but I am a filial child to you"? Would that son be a filial child? No, that is not the case. No matter how it is, that family will perish.

If the one who judges is in a position of suffering and has a higher standard, then they should think about how difficult it is to stand in that place. Do you know how hard that position is? You are in a place of ignorance.

You must walk the path you need to cross. Even if your head is cut off, you must go. Is that not so? That is the case.

The path of faith is to pursue an eternal purpose, so you must walk silently until you find that purpose. Silence precedes action. God does not declare the restoration providence to anyone. Therefore, no one knew this. However, history is advancing toward that limit point, even in ignorance. You must understand this.

You must not forget the attitude of a debtor. If you have no money, you should have a heartfelt, intense feeling that "I am a debtor like this and that," and you must be someone who can hold onto the Father and shed tears. Having such a heart is the correct attitude of a believer.

From the standpoint of a debtor, you must have that heart. When meeting a creditor, do not make excuses, but feel ashamed of your inadequacies and stand in a position where you can bow your head and shed tears; then the creditor cannot urge that person. That is the case. Even if you remain silent, it is so. Ignoring such a person and cutting off their neck will lead to ruin. God will not forgive. Heaven will not forgive.

When you face difficult situations or significant issues in the process of restoration, you must know that you must resolve them, and in the anxiety of that, you must know the difficulties of restoration and strive through sleepless nights to resolve them. Isn't the path of restoration one where you step over each hurdle? Those who bear public responsibilities are struggling in that position, while ignorant fools are criticizing them. That is what destroys their own kind and their ancestors. You must always think about this.

Therefore, the attitude of a believer must be that of a debtor. A single word or a single action done wrong does not only affect oneself. It affects the heavenly realm. The tower built with great effort until now can collapse all at once. If you have spent ten years, that ten years is precious. If you have dedicated your life to the Unification Church until now, the devotion of your youth in those past days is lamentable. However, it is not only lamentable. You must also think it is regrettable. Therefore, you must say, "This is something I cannot give. I must preserve what I have until now. I must leave it behind."

If spring has passed, summer has passed, and you have reached early autumn, you must go until late autumn, and if you have reached late autumn, you must endure until winter. You must go until spring after the winter season has passed. This is how a believer's attitude should be. As you go around once, twice, and three times... There is restoration in going around once, and there is restoration in going around twice... The more you go around, the greater the restoration becomes.

It grows from the individual to the family, tribe, nation, and world. However, this center, this small self, must have the attitude of a believer as a debtor. You must have that attitude. Can someone who offers sacrifices in the age of tribal offerings offer even one sacrifice without the attitude of a debtor? When the age of national offerings comes, can one offer national offerings without the attitude of a debtor? Not a chance.

As the stage becomes increasingly significant and larger, you must understand that the path of faith is to carry the attitude of a debtor.

You may speak in an instant, but if you say one wrong word, it can last for a year. What you said wrong in a moment can take a year to settle.

You must pave the way of suffering and establish the foundation of faith.
Back when I was in prison, I was always hungry, so on the rare days when they served bean rice, that one bean became a golden nugget in the world. It is not just a bean; it feels even more precious than gold. Each bean is more valuable than a lump of gold. If a bean falls while eating, one quickly picks it up without any greeting, without any regard for face. (Laughter) Without any sense of dignity. What I mean is that those who have not been in such a position do not understand. Prison is such a place.

If you think humanly, you want to eat all the food meant for the sinners at once. If there are dozens of prisoners, you want to eat all their food by yourself. You want to eat it all. This becomes an unconscious recognition. When you want to do that, your hand reaches out without you even realizing it. It becomes such an action. Once the desire to reach out and eat arises, you cannot easily eliminate that desire. To atone for that, you have to skip several meals. You must skip several meals to achieve atonement.

From this perspective, it is clear that without God, restoration cannot occur. When I think about how difficult it is to correct a thought that has passed through once, I realize how great God's effort must have been to move fallen humanity from the realm of evil to the position of good. I have come to understand how much energy was consumed.

To lift us, the wicked, to this position, how much effort must God have put in behind the scenes? You should try it too. If you want to, go out and try it. See how much it stimulates and helps you on the path of faith. If your body and mind have made a decision, try it for a lifetime. No matter how new this blackboard is, once you draw a line on it, it is hard to erase. You could spend your whole life trying to erase it. You must feel such things on the path of faith. That is why every single word is so important.

The teacher often admonishes you in public, but do you know how much he worries about your path of faith when he admonishes you? If I admonish you from a position where I can return a million times the admonishment, then my admonishment becomes a blessing for you. In the path of faith, evil must be scraped away repeatedly. It must be scraped away so that it falls off, right? However, good things must not be scraped away. Isn't that so? We must protect goodness through goodness. Evil must be swept away from the side of goodness. That is why the teacher engages in such strategies.

The teacher did not just start off awkwardly to reach that position. That cannot be done. It has been achieved through countless paths of suffering. That is my responsibility, so I cannot help but do it.

Then, what will the one who judges do in the future? They will present it clearly, both internally and externally, theoretically or experientially. You must understand such things.

Even in such trials, He wants to present you, who are equipped, and to love you, hoping to place you in the heavenly kingdom. And then He wants to say, "The restoration you sought is like this, and the image of the servant you sought is not this?" However, to make it so that you can be praised before God, He inevitably has to push you down the harsh path, and who will understand the heart of God's love? When you listen to the words, you will realize, "Ah, I see."

Now, are you in a state of complaint or not? "I am not." Even if the principle is a lie, you must acknowledge it. You must have the right attitude of faith. "The teacher is saying this in front of us because it is everything he wanted to do in his lifetime. Also, it is to set the conditions to help us overcome all the unfair paths before heaven." You should feel gratitude while thinking this.

Let us do our best with the attitude of being indebted. Among the members of our Unification Church, there may be someone who will become a relative of the teacher. Isn't that so? Would you want to become relatives with someone who is good-looking, or with some other people? Have you ever thought about that? If you think deeply, you can have such thoughts. If you want to walk the good path as a good ancestor, you must be able to stand in a position that represents the earth and heaven. From the time of giving birth to a baby, from raising the baby, which family can dedicate themselves with tears and stay up all night in front of God? Wouldn't God look for such families? Are there people with such great aspirations? As the founder of the Unification Church, I think about these things more than I think about being blessed. I think about how to help, and I do not sleep.

Even now, the teacher is like that. When I go to the factory, even if there are people working until midnight, I do not feel sympathy. I work until one or two o'clock. In this busy time, sadness and suffering are not the issues. Can you dedicate yourself without eating, sleeping, or resting? When it comes to dedication, which is more dedicated, not eating and not sleeping, or eating and sleeping? Which is it? Is it more dedicated to do it without eating and sleeping? "Yes, it is." That's it. How can you speak of dedication when you eat when others eat, sleep when others sleep, speak when others speak, and play when others play? Even nowadays, if I sleep at twelve, I wake up at two. Yet during the day, I do not feel tired. I do not even feel a headache. However, when I get in a car, sometimes I fall asleep without realizing it. That happens sometimes. During those times, I pray to God, feeling sorry for falling asleep. In those moments, I feel that God loves me and is with me. Sometimes I wake up startled from sleep. Such things happen continuously. During those times, I exercise. The teacher does special exercises. When I feel tired, I do exciting exercises. I even research exercise to do such things. I will teach you that exercise method in the future.

The teacher thinks about such secrets too. I think about such secrets and work hard. I am already over fifty years old, but I must be like this until I am eighty... When I cross the hardships of two thousand years, I must be like this... I am aiming for the final history. Somehow, it must fit perfectly... There is nothing else in my mind. I have suffered until now. What does it matter if I die? What is there to regret for an old man heading towards the sunset? This is how I think and move forward. Therefore, you must also go with that determination.

The attitude of a believer following the Unification Church today is one that is close to the essence, close to the original form, and can align with the original standard. In terms of your character and all aspects, if you are not praised and admired before heaven, on earth, and even in the spirit world, will the prestige of believing in the Unification Church stand? Think about it. 

When you think about these enormous issues that lie ahead of you, it becomes urgent. If it were me, I would want to turn the world upside down in a day. If I do this and that, it will surely work. It will surely work. If we align like this, the Unification Church will... Because God loves us, He has been preparing the way through the spirit world, guiding us, and bringing us here. Because I know this fact, you must learn to obey.

From this perspective, you must understand the movement of the Unification Church that has been sending out the heads of households in your families since 1971. How urgent is the current situation in Asia? Isn't that right? Therefore, if we have made a decision in our hearts, we must step forward. How urgent is the world right now? The world, South Korea, and our Unification Church are at a critical juncture. If we seize this moment, everything will be resolved.

So look. It is in accordance with the standard of dividing the three offerings. The time has come to divide the offerings on one altar centered on the world situation, the Asian situation, and the Korean situation. The teacher is making the final decisive thoughts on this. Process of Restoration 
Now, I will speak about what position you should take in fulfilling your responsibilities 
centered on the will. 
In saving a nation, the entire nation cannot be restored all at once. The restoration of a 
nation before God begins with one individual. This is the path that God has been guiding 
for 6,000 years. 
So, what process must be gone through for restoration? When we look at fallen humanity, 
the human ancestors Adam and Eve fell, causing humanity to fall into a position of enmity 
before God. The path of restoration is the way to escape that position of enmity and 
reconnect with God to return to Him. 
Therefore, we must understand that the fact that we, who cannot even become servants 
before God, have stood in a position of being a servant of servants is the most blessed 
grace for fallen humanity. From the position of being a servant of servants, we progress 
to the position of a servant. The position of a servant of servants is one that does not have 
a master. The fact that one can progress from the position of a servant of servants to the 
position of a servant, which means being able to welcome a master, is the greatest glory. 
Thus, through the position of a servant of servants, we progress through the position of a 
servant, the position of a child, and finally to the position of a parent, which is the path of 
restoration. 
So, what is the fall? The fall is the failure to establish a family centered on true 
individuals, that is, true sons and daughters. The goal of restoration is to find that 
family that could not be established. What historical changes have occurred until this 
family is restored? It has gone through a long historical process of 6,000 years. 
In this process of restoration history, you must understand that there were those who 
shed tears of blood to fulfill the mission of being servants of servants. 
No matter how much effort one puts in during the age of being a servant of servants, 
even if one dedicates oneself and sacrifices one’s life, one can only be recognized as a 
servant of servants within that era. This is what happens when we enter the Old Testament 
era and begin to fulfill the duties of a servant. Even if one devoted oneself and lived a 
life of sacrifice from the position of a servant during that era, one could not rise beyond 
the position of a servant. 
As we transition from the Old Testament era to the New Testament era, God has promised 
a time when He can welcome His beloved sons and daughters. That promise was the hope of 
tomorrow, which represented the lives of all, and the day when we could welcome God’s 
son became the standard of hope that could replace the lives of all those who lived in faith 
during the age of servants. 
Thus, through the birth of God’s son, that son must go through the process of being a 
servant, then a child, and ultimately establish an unbreakable bond, fulfilling the mission of 
a son and ascending to the position of a parent. By having such a parental relationship, those 
in the position of children can finally receive the benefits of a new inheritance. 
However, even after being faithful as a servant or a child, if one meets a son, one cannot 
establish a position of inheritance from the position of a servant or a child. Only when one 
meets God’s son and completely becomes one with him, allowing that son to fulfill his 
mission as a son and ascend to the position of a parent, can one inherit the position that 
can replace the son’s position. This is the path of restoration.

Moreover, because the tribe is greater than the family, it is a principle that one must sacrifice the family for the tribe. To enter into that, one must sacrifice. Among families that sacrifice, those who pay the greatest sacrifices become the owners. When one family sacrifices first on behalf of the entire family, the countless families will bow their heads before that family that has sacrificed representatively and at the same time will ask it to become their center. 

God knew this principle, which is why He sacrificed His beloved sons and daughters. To always be someone who can remain in that environment, one must become a central being. The center remains. Even if it disappears, the center will only disappear after all the peripheral beings have disappeared. Therefore, when carrying out the restoration history centered on any nation to leave only the center, God's method is to place the most beloved people in the path of suffering. 

At first glance, it may seem like a path to ruin, a path where one may suffer injustice, but after overcoming such a path, that environment will submit before them. This is a principle, and because of this principle, God, who wants to pass on this principled path to children who can remain forever, had no choice but to use this method within the realm of the fallen. 

If you wish to live well, you must not try to live in accordance with the times. 

The same goes for this evangelism period. When asking which family among the 36 families, or 72 families, or 124 families, or 430 families, or 777 families is the one we should emulate, do we say that we should emulate the family that lives well and eats well? When the whole is mobilized, there will be someone who stands at the forefront, treating the difficulties of the whole as their own and struggling to take responsibility for the entire effort. The greater, deeper, and broader the scope of that sacrifice, the more we say that person is worthy of emulation, not someone who, leaving the great aside, runs around seeking only their own comfort. There can be no one to emulate among such people. Is that so? 

Then, how should those who wish to remain or hope to be blessed in the future, those who wish to be good, and those who wish to live well, live? They must understand that they cannot live in accordance with the times. The greater the distance from the times, the more they become a higher person. In this age, if there is someone who looks toward a world that cannot even be dreamed of, someone who lives with such ideals, that person becomes a truly great person. Even if such a person may perish in this world, their thoughts and deeds of goodness will remain forever. Thus, they can surely receive the glory of victory. When that happens, that foundation will be revived once again, and even that person who had died can attain the glory of resurrection. You must understand this fact. Is that not so? 

Jesus died in the face of opposition from the Jews, in the face of opposition from the Israelite people, and in the face of opposition from the Roman authorities, but he never lived a single day centered on the content that could be judged by the Roman Empire, the Israelite people, or Judaism of that time. That is why Jesus was dignified even as he went to the place of death. Even if he was dominated by the times and his body died, his thoughts would become an unshakeable foundation and a central root that could move the world and would not fall short of being the center of the world. Is that not the path of the cross he walked? 

That is why Jesus died in that era but died for the future. "I have sown, so I must reap." "I have become the motivation, so the result must also be mine." Jesus went with that confidence. 

That is why when he comes again to this earth, he will not come from a position of failure but from a position of victory, coming with the authority of goodness before individuals, families, nations, states, and the world. That is why all people must bow their heads before him.

You must say, "I must endure it for more than a hundred years. Since I was born this way, I must die this way." This is the absolute teaching that teaches the eyes, the true teaching. 

Regarding this mouth, you must say, "Oh, you mouth! You have acted as a pump that blows anger into others, haven't you? You must instill hope in those who are despondent. The same goes for your hands and feet. There is no one who has perished by living like that. 

Even a perfect seed cannot produce a tree by just staying as it is. Is that not so? The more perfect the seed, the more it must go into the ground and decay. Only then can grains and trees emerge. A perfect seed, when buried in the ground to die, will instead engage in new activities and burst forth in a second form. Is that not so?

"Yes."

When we see this, how should you live? When there is a saying to go to the North and repay the enemy, if that can be done in about 40 days, perhaps everyone would say they would do it, but if it takes 40 years, they would hesitate and think, "Oh, let me think about it." What you must leave behind through your life

When I walked the path of suffering, I could not utter a single complaint before God because I knew that God worked harder than I did. Even if there were a million times when the heavy cross blocked my way, I knew that God had worked harder than that, so I could overcome the path of suffering as if it were a smooth road and could also overcome trials. Therefore, even if I cannot be the source of strength for you who follow this path I am walking, I must not become someone who drains your strength. This is the heart of the teacher who knows the principles of heaven and has been educated by heaven. In this position, the standard by which the teacher puts in effort must be ahead of your standard.
When you become a parent, you can always be new. You must not become weary after five months. Mobilizing you like this is not to make you live with history. Living well within this historical realm does not leave any gifts for future generations. Even if you shed tears, you must not shed them for your own sons and daughters. Even if you pray, you must not pray for your own sons and daughters. If your longing is deep, that longing should not bear fruit from your blood relations but should bear fruit through the nation. If you cannot do that, you will perish. A woman who leaves her family, starts with a hopeful heart, and thinks of her beloved husband and children as the destination of hope will perish. Such a person will not remain. Such a person will be judged along with history. They cannot cross the boundary of judgment. Furthermore, isn't God's desire to want to stay centered on the world rather than on our family? So, rather than placing my heart on my husband, I should place it on the nation and the world." And you should pray, "Just as I have given my heart to the nation and the world, let me also have a heart that can give to my husband." 

Only then can your husband, although living in the present, be said to be living for the future. And thus, that family will not be a family within the realm of corruption but will become a family that can welcome a future time. You must clearly understand that this is a principled view.

Even when eating, you should not eat for this era. You must eat for the future, for the nation. The same goes for sleeping. You should not sleep for your own comfort. You must sleep to take responsibility for the struggles of tomorrow's nation. Everything you eat, sleep, and do should not be for the current environment but should be done with a firm belief that you are doing it to leave a future tradition.

Who will leave the current tradition of the Unification family as a future tradition? If you try to do it then, it will already be too late. You must understand that without establishing that tradition from now on, you cannot face such a time.

That is why Jesus, when he went up to the Garden of Gethsemane to pray, said, "Abba Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me. Yet not as I will, but as you will." The disciples connected to him were trying to adjust to the environment of the time, and the relatives connected to him were also trying to adjust to the environment, so when viewed from the perspective of emotional connection, he felt himself being drawn into the same position as them. His heart wanted to live with them and fulfill the will with them, but God, knowing that he could not establish the will within the already tilted realm of circumstances, had to move that will to another world, not this one.

The will of God was moved to the future world that Jesus had to go to after his death, not the environment in which Jesus lived. When thinking about the will given to this world in the past, Jesus had a sorrowful heart, saying, "Abba Father! If it is possible... yet not as I will, but..." Here, "as I will" refers to the will he wanted to fulfill centered on that era. Jesus wanted to fulfill his will centered on that era and command the world. However, because the environment to fulfill the will could not be established, God had to place that will in the future. Knowing this, he stood in a conflicting position and prayed three times, groaning and shedding tears of blood, saying, "Not as I will, but as you will." 

At that time, there were many conditions to justify his will centered on his own wishes, but when that will could not be fulfilled in the present environment and was moved to the future, Jesus knew well that complying with that was the way of a filial son of God and a loyal servant, so he prayed, "Not as I will, but as you will."

Even if death and the horrors of the cross were placed before him, that was not the issue. He did not raise the issue of his own personal misery; rather, he thought that if he could not connect the will beyond that hill, then for countless thousands of years into the future, a path of suffering and misery, multiplied by millions, would come upon humanity. Therefore, Jesus did not hesitate to offer his own life as a sacrificial offering on the cross. Under such a resolution, history advanced, and a new era's foundation was laid, which you must clearly understand.

If you cannot fulfill this will alone, what should you do? You must pass on the correct tradition to your descendants. Today, in the Unification Church and the Unification family, you must pass on the correct tradition. Then to whom will you pass it on? In the presence of plus, minus is the counterpart. When looking at today's Unification family, if the center of the Unification family is the teacher, who should you mobilize centered on the teacher? You must mobilize women. Do you understand? Yes. You must mobilize women. When viewed from the perspective of the principle, this cannot be denied.

The significance of mobilizing blessed family women

Because Eve was the cause of the fall, to restore it, women must be the cause. It is the opposite. It is the opposite.

Thus, when you discuss and move with the man on the right side, the archangel will be forced to submit. Isn't that right? If any of you have experience of witnessing in the 60s, you must put in three times the effort you did then. The essence of God's restoration providence
Now, let’s trace the history of restoration starting from Adam's family. Adam and Eve of Adam's family are the parents of two worlds. Because they are the parents of two worlds, Adam and Eve cannot do this or that. Therefore, they fought centered on Cain and Abel. Then Cain killed Abel, right? After that, Cain was afraid. He was afraid that others would kill him. At that time, God said to Cain, "I will punish anyone who kills you sevenfold." What does that mean? Shouldn't God immediately kill Cain, who killed Abel, or punish him in some way? Instead, He said He would give seven times the punishment to anyone who killed him. Did He say He would bless him or punish him? He said He would punish him, right? Then is God on the side of the murderer who killed someone, or is He on the side of those who do not know about the killing? No one has ever asked this question until now.

So why did God make such a paradoxical statement? Think about it. If God had tried to kill Cain, the way to restore the world would have been blocked. God would become the eternal enemy of the world. Do you understand? God and the world would become enemies. Brothers can become enemies, but a father and son cannot become enemies. If they become enemies, the way of restoration will be cut off, and the father-son relationship will also be severed.

Therefore, while the fact that one brother killed another is bad, God, who must leave the providence, could not punish Cain. If He killed him, the providence would be cut off, and everything related to restoration would disappear. Thus, God, who must leave the providence, could not help but think of His will and make opposing statements. Everything is the opposite. Why do you think that is? It is not because of the present but because of the future that He could not help but give such commands.

Look at Grandpa Noah. When Grandpa Noah was building the ark for 120 years, do you think his friends, neighbors, and his mother, father, wife, children, and daughters-in-law liked him? Think about it. Would a father-in-law, carrying a heavy load every day, go out early in the morning and say to his daughter-in-law, "Dear, please prepare the meal early"? Surely he would have said that. He would have urgently told his wife, "Honey, since this old man is going out to work, would it be okay to come back when the sun is high? Please prepare it a bit faster."

Because there was an incredibly long period of 120 years, he might have thought, "I can take it easy for about ten years," but God did not want that. From the day he received the command, He wanted Noah to put in constant effort, to get up earlier than anyone else to start working, to finish later than anyone else, to sleep less than anyone else, and to put in more effort than anyone else.

"Noah, you are not the representative of this era. Therefore, you must establish a tradition that will remain throughout history and align with the providence of restoration. Because you are such a representative, you must establish a tradition that can live with me." God had to say this because He knew that Noah was living a life that did not fit the historical environment, but Noah had to leave a tradition in the course of the providence of restoration that future descendants would follow. Although it may seem miserable and pitiful in itself, God, who could not lose the heavenly kingdom that loved and planned for restoration, wanted to leave him as a co-worker.

Because God cannot align with the reality of the world and is in a position of rejection in the current environment, it was inevitable that He would suffer for 120 years to establish a tradition of faith in the course of human history. Therefore, God told Grandpa Noah to become a beggar of the times, an outcast of the times, and to overcome even in the environment of being pushed away by the times.

In other words, God did not want him to live for that era but to live with the world of the future will that is being revived. Because Noah himself understood that will, he could not avoid pushing his children into a merciless position and could not avoid urging his wife to go into a merciless place. If Noah's wife and children had accepted such recommendations from Noah as a grateful suggestion and viewed what their father was doing as a responsibility they should fulfill, and if they had cooperated with Noah for 120 years, such misfortunes would not have appeared in Noah's family.

However, by complaining and criticizing, Grandpa Noah, who diligently built the ark for 120 years, established a future tradition internally but flowed into the realm of failure without establishing a foundation for actual victory. You must understand this fact.

Grandpa Noah did not live for that era; he lived for the future. Because there was God's will to establish a nation among the peoples that could remain as a higher central nation, he had to live a life that was rejected by the times to leave a tradition that could support the future history. In other words, God made Noah go through such trials to enable him to live with the future.
The Paradoxical Path of Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob

Look at Abraham. He was growing up well under the loving care of his mother and father as the beloved son of an idol merchant, when God called him saying, "Abraham, Abraham! Leave your father's house. Leave Ur of the Chaldeans." This was not a forewarning or a command given in advance. It was a sudden, thunderous command that came down like a bolt from the blue. 

At that time, there was no room for hesitation. When it was time to leave, one had to leave immediately as if they had been waiting for this moment. There could be no saying, "Oh, please wait just a little longer." The departure had to be clean. If the departure was flawed, it would leave a blemish that would haunt history for generations. This would become a condition for Satan's accusations, causing all of history to be denied. Knowing this, those who received the heavenly command acted immediately upon receiving it.

For this reason, Abraham, who received the command, left Ur of the Chaldeans without delay. Can you imagine how bewildered Abraham must have felt? He had to flee at night, leaving behind the beloved mountains and rivers of his hometown, his parents, relatives, and the fun life he had with his siblings. How could he have felt knowing that if his mother and father found out, would they have told him to go? Would his siblings have encouraged him to leave? Thus, he had no choice but to pack his belongings and leave through the front gate while his family was deep in sleep. What must have been going through Abraham's mind at that moment? "Goodbye, mother and father. Take care, my siblings. I am following the path of a divine mission, and surely a miserable road lies ahead of me, with suffering continuing in its wake. But I will surely walk this path and achieve my purpose and return, so please stay alive until then." With a heart torn between conflicting feelings, he prayed for his family's well-being and turned away, setting out on the path of suffering, determined to strategize and resolve to become a warrior for tomorrow. How tragic must have been Abraham's heart at that moment? This is something that cannot be imagined in today's world.

Nevertheless, Abraham executed that command as if he had been waiting for it. His very action was a complete rejection of the idol merchant Terah, that is, the den of Satan, and it was a severing of the death rights. Leaving behind his hometown and family without any lingering attachment was a complete escape from the rights of death. He completely removed and transcended the death rights that surrounded him. You must understand that God commanded such a spectacle.

From the moment Abraham received the command, he became a wanderer, crossing borders into foreign lands, living as a nomad. How miserable must Abraham's life have been? When he entered Egypt, he nearly lost his wife to Pharaoh, and he faced terrible conditions under King Abimelech. Even in the midst of such humiliation, Abraham did not hesitate to send away his wife.

God believed that since the departure was certain, everything else would also be certain. And because he had embarked on a certain path, Abraham believed that to meet that certain day, he must surely overcome all difficulties.

Through this process, Abraham bore Isaac at the age of one hundred, witnessing the evidence that God was with him, and realizing that the promised God was indeed certain, he resolved to go once more. However, it was in this context that the command came down to offer his son as a sacrifice. This was not something that fit the times. In that era, even if such a command were given to anyone, no one would have followed it. All conditions were negative, all actions were negative, and all circumstances were negative. Faced with such conditions, Abraham said, "I am a servant offered before you; how can I go against you, my Master?" With integrity and loyalty, he understood that it was his duty to comply with God's command and walked the path of suffering.

After 120 years of following this path, it was only then that Jacob could establish the foundation for restoration. Thus, by rectifying the mistakes made during Noah's time, the history of restoration could be turned back.

Abraham, Isaac, and Jacob all lived negative lives. Look at Jacob. Could he deceive his brother? So he went to live as a servant in a foreign land. He lived as a servant. He was surrounded by the negative environments of that era, but he was not dominated by them. Though he was like a captive caught in the enemy's encirclement, his heart longed for God and dreamed of the future kingdom of Israel.

Thus, he became the ancestor of the restored world today. Abraham lived such a life, and Jacob did too. To be welcomed in that era would lead to ruin. To wash away the traditions of that time and leave a legacy for the future, one must go through the path of suffering and humiliation. Without doing so, one cannot stand in the place of our ancestors. Is it not our ancestors who have stood in such a path? This is an undeniable fact.

You must understand the purpose behind God establishing the ancestors of faith to walk the paradoxical path. And look at Moses. He grew up in the luxurious palace of Pharaoh as the son of a princess, in a position where he had nothing to envy. Despite being in a position where he should have been loyal to Egypt, he did not lose his integrity towards Israel and set out on the path of labor for his people. The entire nation opposed him, and the whole country became his enemy, yet he stood up for one person, the Israelite. His resolute action, denying the entire nation and its sovereignty for the sake of one Israelite, is not the image of a man with heavenly integrity worthy of praise?

In a position where the entire nation of Israel did not welcome him, he defended one person against the opposition of the whole. To sacrifice his entire self, even risking his life, for the sake of one Israelite was an act that could not be accepted in the social environment of that time.

Thus, our ancestors all paved the foundation of faith through paradoxical actions and methods. That foundation was not laid for that era but was laid to be passed down to us, the descendants of today, so that we can inherit it and carry out the restoration through indemnity. Do you understand what I mean?

Look at John the Baptist. He lived like a wild animal, eating locusts and wild honey, wearing clothes made of camel's hair. What could he have had to wear? After living like that for thirty years, did he have any means? He walked a negative path in such an environment.

So why must those who follow the will of heaven live like that? What is the internal reason behind God's seemingly cruel treatment? If it could have been done without suffering, why didn't He do it that way? It had to be this way because there was no other way to escape the rights of death. This was the quickest route, the secret to solving the problem, and because God knew this secret, He had to lead our ancestors through tears, gritting His teeth, and hearing the groans of suffering until today. You must understand how much God has wept and sacrificed to establish a tradition that can be left for the new future era.

Jesus also walked a different path from the moment He was born on this earth. He grew up differently. Jesus had to marry differently, take a wife differently, and live differently. No matter how hard He worked, He was in a position where the entire social system could not create a different environment, so God, having thought it through, found it impossible and brought Jesus to the point of death to extend the era.

He paid the price of blood to broaden the foundation of restoration. Therefore, Jesus' life was miserable, and His existence was miserable. Who in that era would have been happy to see such a miserable life? Would Jesus Himself have been happy living like that? No. He had to shed tears everywhere He went, run away everywhere He went, and spend nights in deep mountains praying fervently. Who would have wanted such a path? Not a single person in that era wanted it. They all hated it.

However, living such a contradictory life is good, it is true, and because it is the path of following heaven, God made it so. Only then could a single thread of heaven's path be revealed, and a single thread of heaven's tradition be established. Following that tradition, whether as a servant or as sons and daughters, they would leave their marks. Without this, God would not have been able to meet such people, and thus, you must understand that He inevitably sought out a sorrowful and painful path.

Those who wish to follow the Unification Church must understand this internal story.

Therefore, this grace must go beyond the nation and the state to the world. "Go quickly through me." This must be the attitude. Thus, depending on how much you have pushed and developed, your influence can extend throughout the region. You must understand that it will be determined in proportion to your effort.

The correct attitude toward the intention

You have come to the Unification Church and met the teacher, but the steps the teacher has taken to come to you are different from the steps you have taken to come. The reason the teacher sometimes makes you take an oath is to grant you a privileged grace that allows you to stand in the same position as the teacher.

To do this, you must match your steps with the teacher and go over the three hills. Although Arirang Hill is said to be twelve hills, the twelve hills start from the three hills. When looking at the seasons of spring, summer, autumn, and winter, spring is three months. The first hill, the second hill, and the third hill must be crossed. You must go over the three hills. This is like a period of three days. Everything is like this; this three-day period is always a problem.

Then how will you cross these three hills? You must cross the personal hill, the national hill, and the world hill. First, to cross the personal hill, you must abandon your desires and deny yourself.
You are to strike me down. Only then will a smooth path be opened. To cross over the mountain called the nation, you must deny the world of Satan. If denial is not possible, you must strike down and force a denial and submission. Only then can a smooth nation be established. Furthermore, to cross over the mountain of the world, you must deny the world of Satan. If denial is not possible, you must strike down and force a denial. Only then will the world be restored. Do you think you can sleep when you want and eat when you want in this world? Not a chance.
