10)
Sacrifice, Love, and Grace
Everyone, isn’t it nice to pass through safely? When you go to someone’s house, do you look around or not? Are you worried about who might see you? It’s good to think, “It’s okay to be seen.” Is it better to just want to eat more? Passing through safely is good, right? Passing through safely cannot happen without love. Without love, the circumstances and environment for passing through safely do not arise.

Sacrificial Love
When sons and daughters want to sleep in front of their parents, do they say, “Mother, Father, I am ashamed. I am sorry”? That is passing through safely. There is not a single person who dislikes their parents. But why do we like our parents so much? Because parental love is unconditional love, sacrificial love, and serving love.

When people usually say, “That woman suffered so much before getting married, but she married well,” what kind of man do they mean when they say she married well? It means she married a man who loves her unconditionally, day and night. If there is ever a mistake, he would say, “I was wrong,” and he would take full responsibility for loving his bride. If that bride became the wife of such a man, did she marry well or not? Answer me. Did she marry well or not? “She married well.” Surely she married well, right? “Yes.” If the husband can give such sacrificial love to his wife, did that husband marry well or not?

Then, do you want your mother to do that for your father or not? That is also part of growing up. Do you want your father to give sacrificial love to your mother or not? When parents give and receive sacrificial love, who benefits from that? Who benefits? The sons and daughters desire that. When parents get along well, that good relationship becomes a blessing for the sons and daughters. The environment of the sons and daughters improves. Isn’t that right? If the two can do that, the sons and daughters will be blessed abundantly. That is truly wonderful. There is nothing in the world to envy.

When we look at it this way, what is the greatest blessing among blessings? It is to give sacrificial love, serving love, and love for others. Do you understand? Love for oneself does not last long. Isn’t that right? When a husband sees that his wife is gentle… Are there gentle young women here? Even if they are gentle in appearance or heart, if you poke them once, twice, three times, or four times, they can get upset… (As he acts it out, everyone laughs)

If those gentle women only love for themselves, they will look around and compare, and it will become… oh dear… a desolate situation. They might think, “Women are born pitifully.” Would you think that way or not? What, is a woman some kind of plaything or accessory for a man? Even if she is an accessory, she must move in sync to fulfill her role. What is this? Love for oneself may seem good at first, but it will surely lead to separation. Will it separate or not? It will separate.

You have husbands, right? Try saying this to the husband who says he loves you. “What are you? What are you? What kind of man’s love is that? You should do more for me. Since you are a man, you should love me more. Let’s fight once.” (Laughter) Try that and see how your husband reacts. (Laughter) Do you hear that in the back? “Yes.” Love centered around oneself leads to disaster. Isn’t that right? However, if a new husband continues to love his new bride like that, it will not lead to disaster. Do you understand?

Where is the location of love?
Therefore, when we ask where the location of love is, it concludes that it is not “me.” When we ask where the location of true love is, it is the bride in front of the husband and the husband in front of the bride. Is the location of love oneself or the other? It is the other. There is a principle of heaven and earth in this. That is why there is a counterpart.

Because the location of love is the counterpart, one must bow their head to the other and say, “I wish,” in order to receive love. That is the principle. Do you understand? Therefore, only when one serves, sacrifices, and acts for others can love move and thrive from its original location. Do you understand?

Where is the location of love? “It is the counterpart.” Because the location of love is the counterpart, one cannot say it is their love until they completely occupy the counterpart. Saying “my bride, my husband” is stimulating. Young people must say it that way to make it exciting. Saying “my husband, my wife” does not have the same flavor. It has to be “my bride, my husband.” (Laughter)

To say “my love,” one must completely occupy the counterpart. Until then, it cannot be called “my love.” Isn’t that so? If a husband says to his wife, “I am so great that a woman like you is destined to love me. A woman who cannot love me is not a woman,” he may be listened to once or twice, but if he keeps saying that, she will want to retaliate, and she will want to test him. That is the heart of a woman. Isn’t that so? That is how it is. Therefore, one must clearly understand that the location of love is not oneself. Do you understand?

When we say we love our country, where is the location of that love? Is it within oneself? It is in the country. When we say we love the world, where is the location of that love? It is in the world. Then, how can we make that love our own? We must serve for the world. Among all who serve, if there is someone who actively steps forward and is willing to give their life, that person will first establish a connection of love.

To receive the gift of love
When a young woman prepares herself to get married and waits with pure intentions, thinking, “What kind of husband will appear?” and then receives a proposal from a handsome man from a neighboring town, would she feel good or bad? Women, would you feel good? Women would feel bad because they think, “Who can I trust to reveal the bundle of pure intentions I have kept hidden?” Would you trust those thieving men? Even if someone proposes, she would feel bad.

So, everyone, would you feel bad? When you hear someone wants to marry you, would you feel bad or good? If a young woman does not know what marriage is, she might not understand, but if she knows what marriage is and has the desire to marry, she would feel disappointed if no one wants to marry her. However, if she wants to marry and someone comes to propose, would she feel good or bad? I don’t know because I am not a woman. Ladies, answer me. Would you feel good or bad? “Good.” It would feel good.

Feeling good, she would become curious about that person. When she wakes up in the morning, she would think it would be nice to meet that man. The man she envisions has certain qualities; she would wonder how many of those qualities the man who proposed has. If that man meets or exceeds her expectations when they first meet, she would wish to hold onto him and dance with joy.

Would she wish for someone who is less than what she desires or someone who exceeds her desires? The desire is for someone who exceeds her expectations. Isn’t that right? 

However, if three such men appear at the same time, would she want to see just one or all three? “All three.” There are many desires. Then what if a hundred men appear at once? “In that case, I would just close my eyes and choose one.” Is that right? If a hundred men appear and say they want to marry her, would she have to meet each one or could she skip meeting some? Even if she meets one every three days, it would take a year.

If she meets all those hundred men and rejects one, ten, thirty, or sixty, will the remaining men stick around? (Laughter) The ones who remain would be foolish. If she has rejected sixty, the others will run away. Even the sixtieth will run away. That is possible, isn’t it?

“How could that woman have rejected all those fine men… Where is she planning to marry? Oh, what a shame!” (Laughter) That could happen. Therefore, one must start well. If one does not start well, they will fail. Even pure intentions can be ruined if the start is wrong.

So how should one go about getting married? How should one get married? For someone seeking sacrificial love… Think about it. To love someone who is not good-looking, one must put in more effort than others, so sacrificial love is necessary. If sacrificial love is happiness, then loving with double the sacrifice is a greater blessing than loving with single sacrifice.

If God exists, when giving good sons and daughters, if there is a couple who lives well with one unit of effort and another couple who live just as well but with a less attractive husband who puts in double the effort, whom do you think God would want to give good sons and daughters to? Even I, as God, would want to give good sons and daughters to the couple who lives well with double the effort. Isn’t that the heart of God?

Why is that? Because the gift of love must be based on greater sacrifice. Since the essence of love is sacrifice, only with that foundation can one receive the blessed children to leave for future generations.

If one has that mindset, what should they do? If a hundred men come, instead of looking for the best, one should say, “If you are a man, you should be ready to love me at any time, day or night. If you want to marry me, compete among yourselves, and the last man standing will come to me.” That is how a woman should be. Then the men will think, “Wow, that woman is amazing!” and they will compete among themselves.

When they ask each other, “Are you going to marry that woman? Are you really going to?” and one says, “Yes,” the other might say, “Really? Are you going to fight me for her? Come on. I’m already prepared to risk my life.” If someone charges in without even looking at the others, in the end, only two men will remain. They will fight and chase away everyone else, and in the end, the one who remains will be the one who is ready to give their life. In this way, even if one does not see the man beforehand, they will still end up marrying well. Isn’t that so?

But what if it turns out he is cross-eyed? Have you thought about a cross-eyed husband? “No.” If that were the case, what would happen? If a young woman promised to marry the last man standing after a fight, should she marry him even if he is cross-eyed or should she not? “She should marry him.” If she does not marry that person, she will become a woman worse than a widow. She will not be able to marry.

If a girl enjoys watching the fight among a hundred men and does not take it seriously, she will not be able to marry. 

If she made a promise, even if that person is cross-eyed, she must marry him. Try marrying a husband who serves. Even if he cannot see, his love will be the strongest. Isn’t that so? When you think about it, not being able to see does not mean being unhappy. Not having one leg does not mean being unhappy either.

Love is something one wants to leave behind forever, right? Isn’t that so? Love is something one wants to leave behind forever. Truth is eternal. Happiness is thought of that way. If we keep talking like this, there will be no end.

True love is based on sacrifice.
The location of happiness is love, but where is the location of love? It is not oneself. Therefore, to love one’s country, one must risk their life for the country. Do you understand? The same goes for loving the world. To possess that love, to receive the blessings of that love, one must be willing to give their life. Love that does not risk life is not true love.

That is why even an eighty-year-old grandmother would do anything to extend her beloved husband’s life for even three days, even if it means sacrificing her own body. Only with such a heart can we say that their love is true love. One must understand that true love is based on sacrifice. True love is something everyone likes, right? You must clearly understand this.

You have probably never heard Reverend Moon of the Unification Church stand on a podium and say, “Live well and eat well. Live plump like a pig or a cow.” Have you heard that? Have you not heard? This is because those who suffer for others gain love. Do you understand? When you work hard for others, there is something you will definitely receive in return for that effort, and that is the love of that person.

(While writing on the board) And when that neighborhood comes to support me, it becomes a report for that neighborhood, gradually jumping up. The Unification Church is the most miserable group that has been criticized by the Korean people and the Korean religious community in recent times. There is no other religion that is as miserable as the Unification Church. If there is a most miserable person, it is none other than the members of the Unification Church who lead such a miserable religion. That is why God is a pitiful being.

God is working so hard to establish the laws of justice, and with a heart that pours out sincerity toward the world regarding the will of justice, while standing on the lonely street where He suffers and is persecuted, looking at the sun setting in the west, no one knows that behind the lonely believers who worry about their sleeping arrangements and evening meals, the light of Heaven’s compassion is hidden. You must know this.

You must not forget that you are standing in a position where you can receive blessings that cannot be exchanged for anything, standing on the foundation of the hard work of those who have gone through the history of groans and death on the three thousand ri peninsula.

You must not forget that you are standing on the foundation of the hard work of those who have gone through the history of groans and death on the three thousand ri peninsula, where the sorrow of countless beings is intertwined, and that you are the ones who have come to find a day of hope.

You have been born in an incredible era and have been called in a unique connection that happens only once. You must understand that the hyperbolic curve of the flow of history, which has never existed before and will never exist again, intersects at the peak of your lifetime.

Even if the history of the fall in the six thousand years of human history has been sorrowful and full of twists and turns, because today this tangled humanity has not been conquered, a historical resurrection remains within this ideology, and God’s sorrow and grief can be resolved here. When you think that this is the origin that can solve all the affairs of the nations, you should be proud above all else that you were born in such a time.

Your own face is nothing, and your own appearance is nothing, but you must recognize that you are the representatives who receive the grace that your ancestors wanted to receive on behalf of the whole, as Heaven comes to help you according to the connection of your ancestors’ achievements that shine for eternity.

Although the history of groans and death has been woven on the three thousand ri peninsula, you must understand that the Unification Church, where you stand today, is a place where all of that can be forgiven at once, and where you can receive blessings that cannot be exchanged for anything.

Do not forget that you are in a blessed position.

Meeting the Teacher is not a coincidence. It is through the inevitable path of historical destiny that this internal connection has been determined and met. You may not know it, but there is an undeniable force behind it. Something is rooted in this.

In this mobilization of women, there may be those who resist being mobilized, those who complain in their hearts. However, when you look back at those who are being mobilized, if you feel a force that makes you unable to endure not going out, where does that force come from? It comes from the heavenly fortune that God wanted to leave behind, which must remain forever in history, and from the heart and feelings of God’s wishes. This is what acts as the force that can push your environment.

When you think about this, you must realize that the position you are in, mobilized by this force, is a blessed position that can be more grateful than receiving all the blessings of heaven and earth. Anyone living in such a position, suffering from the pain of conscience, will be punished. If God has commanded you to awaken and respond internally, but you do not match that, you will perish.

In this amazing historical era, the path the Teacher walks is not a smooth one, and when you think that the suffering the Teacher has endured cannot be compared to what you have faced in your lifetime, you must fulfill your duties of filial piety and loyalty. Yet, what is your standard of filial piety? You have received teachings, but you have not yet practiced what you have learned. You are in a position where you have been commanded to go out to the battlefield to fulfill your heavenly mission, but you have not gone out! Do you think you can establish your dignity like that? If that is the case, it would be better to die.
In this way, being unable to take care of oneself and unable to uphold one's dignity is a pitiful state. However, knowing that God has taken responsibility and allowed this moment to establish dignity and prestige is an invaluable gift. It is essential that the hope of heaven can come upon your steps as you walk, or that the news of heaven can sprout in the place where you stay. When that happens, you will begin to prosper from there. From this perspective, you must understand that the most astonishing gift, indeed the greatest miracle, is nothing other than this.

The teacher you meet in such a relationship, and the sons and daughters born from the relationship with your husband centered on the teacher, are not just coincidental children; they are historical children. When you look at these historical sons and daughters, when they shed tears, or when they are mocked and ridiculed by the children of the satanic world in lonely places on the streets, it will not be in vain.

All of these experiences will broaden your path, alleviate your lonely journey, and thus prepare a pure offering that can be presented before heaven on behalf of the nation. When you think this way, leaving behind your lonely sons and daughters can indeed be a blessing, and leaving behind your beloved husband can also be a blessing.

You must be able to pour your heart into the nation and the cause, dedicating every moment. This is a place where you cannot see the husband and the sons and daughters you long to see, so the more your longing does not cease, the more it will give rise to sacrificial love for heaven, and the foundation of sacrificial love for heaven will expand. Therefore, the foundation that the Unification Church must establish today, by paying the price of sacrifice, will open the way to extend beyond the nation and people to the world. When you think of this, you must not forget that the position we are in today is a blessed one.

Love the nation and the world more than your own sons and daughters. You, as a weak and fragile woman, have reached a time when you can love your nation more than General Yi Sun-sin. You are in a position where you can show more filial piety than anyone else in loving your parents, and you are in a position to create connections of sacrifice, love, and grace that can love the world. Do not forget that you are in a time when you can fulfill a comprehensive mission and responsibility that has only happened once in history, and I hope you will diligently pay the price of effort with sincerity.

You should feel ashamed even after waking up early in the morning, and you should have the desire to convey the word even if you go to bed late. Just as one does not realize how late it is when meeting someone they miss and love, you should be able to long for and love.

In the position of wanting to love someone who is in a relative position to your beloved sons and daughters, and wanting to give and care for them as if you were crazy, if you spend the night praying in that place, even if God is far away, He will be with you, and the countless spirits in the spiritual world, despite the historical gap of thousands of years, will be able to resonate with you in the emotional world, supporting your path and standing in a position to uphold your purpose.

You must understand that the holy path today, where history is turning and all the fortunes of the world can turn with you, is the path you are taking to work hard for this nation and people globally. Therefore, you are encouraged to invest your sincerity for the nation, to love more than your husband, and to love more than your sons and daughters for the world. Even if you forget your husband and children before 360 days pass, if it is for the nation and the world, those children and husband will not suffer. Even if you find yourself in a position where you might starve to death, you will not die. You absolutely will not die.

The grace you can receive in the Unification Church is a grace that will remain for tens of thousands of years, and it is the only grace that has happened only once in history. To receive such grace, how much sacrifice and effort must you pay? How much sincerity must you put into it?

The reason the teacher strives before you is that he does not want to owe you anything. He is trying to avoid incurring a debt. If I were to place you in a position of suffering while I seek comfort for myself, that would lead to ruin. Such a group would perish. If God does not make us suffer and does not take responsibility, then that God would perish. This is the place where we can make God suffer even more.

You must understand that the Unification Church is in a position to help God find value in His suffering and willingly stand in a position where He can regard that suffering as worthwhile. You must know that the way to alleviate the suffering of God who groans in suffering and to liberate Him begins from here. Suffering must be compensated with suffering as a principle. When you suffer, if God can say, "My child, that’s enough. I would gladly die a hundred times for you," then wouldn't the world turn upside down?

You should not avoid the path of suffering but rather take on more suffering on behalf of heaven. When you step forward with a heart that clings to a hungry belly, dragging your weak legs and exhausted body, crying out as a fragile woman, at that moment, God's will will take root deeply, and the heavenly providence that connects the world beyond the nation will ripple through you and extend to the world. It is akin to a broadcasting station. Just as the waves broadcasted from a station spread throughout the universe, when you stand in a position where you can be the pulse and control the origin of life and death, fulfilling such a mission is an incredibly astonishing fact.

Act as one. When will you stand in such a position? When you, whether a thousand or eight hundred of you, unite as one and offer grace over a period of three years that surpasses what women in historical times have offered, historical women will surely be embraced in our arms and will naturally kneel before us. Isn’t that so? Therefore, you must understand that it is not just 120 but 1,200 that we mobilize as a standard.

It is difficult for ten people to become one. Is it easy for you to unite? Therefore, the first step is for you ten to become one. Unite and teach the district leaders and regional leaders that you have become one in such a way that they can follow your tradition. The Unification Church has been ruined because the district and regional leaders could not do that.

They have exploited, used, and drained the members, causing them to flee. Since all the members have been chased away, what must be done to gather them again? If you do not do the work of sacrificing yourself to nourish them, members will not be born.

Who must do that? When a mother raises her children, does she not share her own flesh? The mother’s flesh should be connected to the father’s bones. Otherwise, that flesh becomes excess fat. From this perspective, women’s emotional depth and height of affection are greater than men’s. Therefore, when you are equipped on all sides and become sincere, even if a man cries once, a woman will cry three times.

In this light, it is only natural to elevate women in a position that requires a lot of compensation for indemnity and a lot of effort for that indemnity. Therefore, you must take on this responsibility and do your utmost to prevent the fate of this nation from perishing.

It is a miracle that this nation has survived for half a millennium of history. This is because there was a foundation laid by our ancestors to prepare for a certain time. Today, we are in a position to bear fruit in our time, and with the determination not to leave suffering for future generations, even if we become dry and fall, we must go out with the resolution that we cannot return until this purpose is fulfilled. If you say, "Oh, I can’t stand it anymore," that matter will drag on indefinitely. You must understand this and unite as ten. You must become one with the district and regional leaders.

Where is the foundation of love? You must treat each other as the source of love, and that love must seek the source of love on earth or in the nation, allowing roots to spread. To do this, you must give water; if there is no water, you must sprinkle tears and blood in place of water, which is the position of the children of heaven. Therefore, you must know that you cannot remain without paying the price of sacrifice, and since you have already taken this step, you must walk this path.

Why do you walk this path? To leave grace behind. If you wish to receive a thousand years of grace, you must overcome the path of a thousand years of suffering. If you wish to walk the path of ten thousand years of grace, you must overcome the path of ten thousand years of suffering. The Unification Church has only suffered for about twenty years, and the teacher has only suffered for about fifty years. This is far too little to compensate for all the paths of suffering. Therefore, you must feel the responsibility to go and keep going.

The amount of burden one person must carry is predetermined. If it exceeds that amount, it becomes excessive. If it becomes excessive, everything will come to an end. God knows this very well. Therefore, if you do more than the amount you are responsible for, God will take responsibility for you. God will try to impose a debt on you beyond that. Parents do not want to incur debts before their children but rather want to impose debts on them. Therefore, if you do this for God, He will take on that burden for you, and even if you want to work, He will not allow you to do so and will prepare a resting place for you. This is God's love.

When you think of this, when you work hard for this nation and country, if it can become something that God cannot bear and cannot endure with gratitude, then your nation will surely return quickly as you desire. Do you understand what I mean?

Be grateful that you are walking a more blessed path than the prophets. When you go out to work in the regions, I am at the headquarters, but I have a deep desire to visit you. I do not want to incur a debt because I know the distance. However, it is too difficult to travel from the base in Seoul all the way to the southern sea. It is too time-consuming to go beyond the provinces to find you. Although I cannot visit, I am well aware of the suffering and pain you endure.

Therefore, just as I have been guided by God when I stood in sorrow, when your daughters are in such sorrow, you must treat them with even more heart than you have treated me. You must also appeal to God to allow me to have a heart of cooperation, comfort, and compassion for them. This is undoubtedly the fact you must understand.

For this reason, even while you are working hard, the desire to resent the teacher should never arise in your dreams. Why? Because your heart knows this. I have walked the path of suffering until now, but I cannot have a heart to resent God because I know how much He loves me.

When I stepped onto the path of death, prepared to die, I think of how God unknowingly placed me in a position of peace many times over. Thus, being on the path of suffering is not a bad thing. That path is the way to inherit the blessed standard that cannot be reached without suffering. Therefore, to become a more blessed Unification Church and a more blessed you, you must inevitably walk such a path.

Here, all kinds of sacrificial love from the teacher must be bound together, and your sacrificial love must also be bound here. This love, where the teacher cares for you and you care for the teacher, is for whom? It is for the nation. Therefore, with this love, bind together the three thousand ri peninsula and the hearts of thirty million people. When you cry out centered on the love you exchange with the teacher, thirty million people will bend and break. When they break and cannot communicate, they will be cut off.

If any of you do not have a grandfather, you should be grateful that you can now have one and that you can meet him to understand his circumstances. There are many grandfathers in the neighborhood. There are many grandmothers, aunts, uncles, mothers, and many brothers and sisters.

From this perspective, you must think that Jesus could not love his father, grandfather, grandmother, mother, or siblings, and you have become a wife and bride who is expanding the foundation of love to bring such a Jesus to represent this nation. You should love the grandfather you meet in place of Jesus' grandfather, with the heart to fulfill the longing Jesus had to love his grandfather. You must love.

Who is the representative brother who can love our nation? It would be the grandfather, uncle, older brother, or younger brother. If we speak of men, that is the case. If we speak of women, it would be the grandmother, aunt, older sister, or younger sister. These are the eight types of brothers. You are loving these eight figures on behalf of humanity. Gather them together and say, "Oh, humanity, pay attention to me," or "Oh, thirty million people, pay attention to me," or "Oh, citizens and residents, pay attention to me." Select these eight representatives and before them, say, "I will set up a standard that I have loved with all my sincerity; please contribute to establishing this standard."

If there are any satanic elements opposing this, you must block them. When you stand in a position saying, "Even if I die, I will surely establish this purpose," and if your own strength is insufficient, remember that there are ten supporters beside you who can cooperate. Are you not better than the Holy Spirit? The Holy Spirit has been working with Jesus to find children until now, but you have stood in a position where ten people can unite around the teacher to find children and love the nation. Even if persecution is severe, it should not be too difficult to overcome! You have someone who can shed tears for each other, and you can share love with one another.
Because you are in a position to encourage others, you should be grateful that you are walking a blessed path compared to the ancient prophets. (The following is not recorded) *

Establishment of Traditional Thought
<Summary of the Message> What does "will" mean? The will is for the world and for future generations. Is the fulfillment of God's will centered on the Republic of Korea? It is for the world. Is it only for the present? Even if the present perishes, it is for future generations. 

Those who are satisfied with the present and sing and dance in happiness are nearing their end, but those who harbor hope for the future and overcome the present will find a bright tomorrow. This is the teacher's thought. I have not yet grown weary. You must understand this. 

The teacher is truly astonishing. It is to the point of being overwhelming. Despite pouring all kinds of sincerity into you, it is overwhelming. There is a saying that one should not break a bowl even if they cannot give alms or cooperate; isn't it similar? At this critical juncture of crossing the final threshold, should we not support you to cross, but rather pull you down? 

A priest should not have the concept of ownership or existence.
Look at your families. You are archangels. Then what position do your wives hold? They are not in the position of completion but rather in the position of growth. 

Centered around your families, we have mobilized 1,200 people in the Korean Peninsula. This is a global matter. (Omitted) 

As original sons and daughters, we must set conditions not to betray God, and we are currently doing this work centered around 1,200 people. Originally, we were supposed to start this journey from the first day of the lunar new year in 1970. However, the teacher set the condition to go on a special three-year journey, so we started on the first day of December. I sympathized with you in that way. Whether the teacher did this or not, go check in the spirit world. Do you know which direction the will is heading? Do you think the will of heaven will be easily fulfilled according to your thoughts? 

It will be the same in the future. Now, speak up. Let’s talk openly. If anyone thinks the teacher is wrong, speak up. I mean, speak from a principled standpoint. 

The teacher wants to give all of you a salary. I want to budget and give you a salary, but I cannot do it from a principled standpoint. Why can’t I? To budget, I must first set the budget for the teacher's household. It is a principle that the president uses the taxes of the country, not that he earns directly and spends. Is there such a principle? 

First, the budget for the teacher's household must be set, and then sequentially for the headquarters, the victory alliance, and the factory. When looking at the Republic of Korea, it is a principle that the budget for the Blue House must be secured first, and then sequentially budgeted around the government. But have you set the foundation for that? This is the problem. 

I do not think that everything planned will be achieved 100%. The teacher told you what you should do for a year on the first day of the lunar new year, but when we check the results at the end of the year, nothing has been done properly. Everything falls under conditions. It is not that the teacher does not know how to plan and organize work. The teacher's mind is organized. Do you think I want to do it haphazardly? 

We must conduct guerrilla warfare in front of the whole. If you cannot budget for the first and second quarters, it is the simplest way to hold you accountable. No one can oppose that. 

Those within our church organization must be paid a salary. However, district leaders should not think about receiving a salary. Is a priest someone who thinks about receiving a salary? District leaders should understand that even if the reward for their sacrifice of shedding blood and cutting flesh is small, it is a price that can shake heaven and earth. That is the traditional thought centered around the Bible. 

What is a priest? A substitute for the offering. Because they are living offerings, they should not have the concept of ownership. If you have the notion of wanting to possess something, you cannot be an offering. If you think, "I am someone's son," or "I belong to a certain tribe," you cannot be an offering. 

Furthermore, there should be no consciousness of existence. You must go in a position where you can reflect on yourself and feel regret for not fulfilling your mission. You must understand that the path to heaven is one where you bow your head more and more as you go. 

You must put in sincerity. You must shed tears, blood, and sweat. That is the teacher's traditional thought. (Omitted) 

The path of those called before the will
From now on, the remaining journey of the teacher will become the genealogy of the tradition that you must establish throughout your lives. Therefore, you must receive education again. I often speak to the Japanese members about things I have not said to you. Otherwise, wouldn’t I lose everything to the Japanese members? 

From this principled perspective, was this family arrangement done well or not? Answer me. Do you need to hear the teacher's explanation to answer? What kind of filial child is that? What kind of loyal subject is that? The time has come when it should not be like that, which is why this year I am paying more than 2,000 won a day to solve the church problem. I also expect that the factory will get through this year, but above all, what is important is that you unite and become one. Shouldn't the direction of your hearts be unified? 

What will you do without the teacher? Who is there to take responsibility in place of the teacher? Everyone is pitiful. The association president is pitiful, and all of you gathered here are pitiful. Have you ever thought about that? Therefore, we must raise people. Aren’t you all lonely people? 

Even while you live difficult lives, when you report to the teacher that someone is having a hard time, you want to willingly give money with a joyful heart. 

If you look closely at the Bible, there are many questions. In Genesis, God said that anyone who kills Cain, who killed his beloved Abel, will receive a sevenfold punishment. Yet none of you have asked about that point. 

Noah built the ark for 120 years. Noah must have been laughed at by the people of his time as a crazy man. Abraham, who was about to sacrifice his only son, Moses, who ran away from the palace, and John the Baptist, who lived in the wilderness eating locusts and wild honey for 30 years, would they have been praised by the people of the world? The people of the world must have all laughed at them as crazy. Even their parents would not have praised them for doing well. 

It had nothing to do with normal life. 

But why did they do that? You must understand that. If Cain were to die after Abel, the restoration providence could not be fulfilled. There must be a counterpart. If that happens, everything will collapse. Therefore, he had to be left alive. 

Think about Noah, who built the ark for 120 years. Wouldn’t it have been better if Noah had built the ark by the sea instead of on a mountain? By building it on a mountain instead of by the sea, everything was denied. Then what did Noah live for? Noah lived for the future. He established a tradition of living for the future in his time. 

In the same way, even if living within the realm of death, one must establish a historical tradition that can penetrate that realm of death and enter the realm of life in the future, so that the foundation of the future's will can be expanded and the will can remain. That is why God made them live negatively in the real world. 

Abraham was the same. It was not to be welcomed in that era. In that era, it was denied, but there was no way to escape the world of death without establishing a historical tradition for the providence of the future. Therefore, God entrusted them with the responsibility of salvation to create a path to cross the realm of death. 

The history of the restoration providence has all been carried out in that way. Moses was the same. What did Moses, who grew up in the luxurious palace of Pharaoh, envy? However, he stood on the side of the Israelites, who had to regard his own kin and the heavenly lineage as enemies. That is the traditional thought of heaven. 

This thought may be denied in this age, but it will remain in the world of the future. John the Baptist had this thought, and Jesus was the same. The teacher is also the same. The teacher does not live for this age. The teacher is absolutely not someone who adjusts to your feelings and lives happily for this age. (Omitted) 

Reflect on yourself and establish traditional thought
The teacher is doing things that you do not know. However, if you really want to know, I can tell you everything openly. But you must take responsibility. You must leave a tradition. 

That is why this year we have the slogan "Securing the Unification Foundation." Do you know what "securing the unification foundation" means? The time that can remain in the end is being established today centered around our unification group. It is truly astonishing. 

When you stand on the platform with the title of district leader, don’t your legs tremble? Have you never felt that? Imagine that you are responsible for the lives of these members. When the teacher stands on the platform to say something significant, he thinks that way. It was so serious that I did not even know if my feet were touching the ground. 

That is why heaven is with us. It is not oneself who goes up to the platform. It is like a doctor treating a critically ill patient. When using the final secret to give a good injection, what would that feeling be like? Hands would tremble, and all nerves would be concentrated. Heaven advances history in such places and forms connections in such places. 

But do you think the will will be fulfilled with such an attitude as yours? Critically reflect on yourself. What will you do without the teacher? Can everyone just separate? Where will you go with your children at that time? Think about it. You must understand that. Therefore, even without the teacher, there must be someone who can take the teacher's place. You must be able to think about such things. 

A true loyal subject is one who does not only serve a single king but also pleads to serve the kings of thousands and tens of thousands for the nation. 

It is easy to be a district leader of the Unification Church or the president of the Unification Church when the teacher is present. (Omitted) 

If I were in your position and sincerely believed that the teacher is the responsible person for the true will, I would not act like you. I would take a risk. I would take a risk to see if heaven truly supports me. You must be able to think that far. 

In the 1960s, the teacher blessed you while going to the court to prepare documents. He worked hard to save you, but what is the result? 

With your current attitude, nothing will work. If it seems possible, I would welcome it with both hands. You must remember that you need to adjust your attitude again during this opportunity. (End) *
